The others have also exceeded my expectations; keep up the good work. As someone once said, I have an extremely thick skin…”

Before Chen Ping'an could finish, Gu Jianlong, while watching the situation, urgently exclaimed, “Hidden Official, may I speak fairly?!”

Chen Ping'an smiled and said, “Scram.”

Gu Jianlong sighed, “Hidden Official, you truly are magnanimous!”

Chen Ping'an waved his hand and said, “In the next minute, find twenty earth demon cultivators. Under the premise that it does not interfere with the overall situation, let’s provide the sword immortal seniors with some easily obtainable military merits. You all should discuss and come up with a list of specific targets from both sides, and once confirmed, send flying swords to our sword immortals. Meanwhile, there’s another matter: who here knows how to use the similar stele expansion technique? You’ll be responsible for duplicating the eleven volumes I have compiled aside from the Ji Ben, ensuring each person has a copy on their desk. This matter can take its time.”

Cao Gun chuckled, “I can do it.”

Chen Ping'an then took the eleven books from his desk and moved them to Cao Gun’s table, squatting beside him to share his insights in a whisper. Cao Gun focused intently, occasionally nodding or asking a question or two.

An hour later.

The great demon Huang Luan, who was sitting on the railing with Yang Zhi, said, “I really want to curse.”

Yang Zhi was filled with intense rage; her two subordinate armies at the flanks of the magical artifact flood often suffered losses of several earth immortals with a single sword light detour. After multiple instances, the losses were significant. This wasn’t the most infuriating part, however; what truly made her anxious and pained was how the sword immortals of the Sword Qi Great Wall only maintained gaps in the sword formation, repeatedly doing so “casually!”

The precision and ruthlessness of those sword immortals’ strikes were as if someone on the barbaric world was leaking information.

The peak great demon, who still bore guilt, had originally been able to intercept and kill the disruptive sword immortals in the barbaric world. However, at this moment, she could no longer sit still and lacked the face to leave the battlefield. She stood up and gazed toward the city wall, her anger boiling, “What the hell is going on?!”

“Fishing again, Yang Zhi, but you might bait the wrong hook; how about we join forces?” 

Huang Luan pointed toward a spot on the city wall where Lu Zhi stood; next to the female sword immortal was a young man holding a folding fan.

Yang Zhi looked over at Lu Zhi. 

If she acted recklessly and attacked the city wall alone, she might not return. But if she teamed up with Huang Luan, they should be safe. Even if they couldn’t gain much, it was unlikely they would be blocked by the Sword Qi Great Wall.

So just as she was about to agree, the young man beside Lu Zhi suddenly seemed to look their way.

He raised his hand high, beaming with a bright smile, and extended his middle finger. Not only that, but he also seemed to utter three words with his lips.

“F*** your mother.”

*(End of Chapter)*

 ### Chapter 739: Huang Luan Proposes a Joint Journey to the Sword Qi Great Wall

The proposal from Huang Luan to embark on a joint expedition to the Sword Qi Great Wall was indeed tempting. The sword formations of the Great Wall were intricately connected, leaving nearly no idle swordsmen. Standing on the railing, Yang Zhi had already dispelled her illusions, revealing her kingly demeanor with the imperial crown and a flowing dragon robe. 

Yet, Yang Zhi did not act immediately. Instead, she gazed at the young man atop the city wall and asked Huang Luan, “Is the sword immortal on the city wall the one directing the sword formations? How can he possess such skill? Isn’t he just an outsider traveling the Sword Qi Great Wall? When did the reputation of the Scholar of the Way of Righteousness become so grand? I’ve heard that Lu Zhi has never had a good impression of scholars.”

Earlier, when Chen Ping'an fought against the direct disciple of the Grand Master of the Moon Trampling Mountain, all the great demons atop the wild mountains observed leisurely, their eyes fixed on the scene. However, at that time, ancient beings like Yang Zhi did not think this slightly larger ant had any ability to influence the course of the battle. In a confrontation between the entire world and the Sword Qi Great Wall, even sword cultivators of the Fifth Realm were not indispensable. The three sword immortals of the Great Wall had fallen as easily as stones, merely stirring up a splash of water.

Once, a great demon who had attacked the city returned grievously wounded, ultimately disappearing into the endless river of time, laughing and expressing heartfelt words before his demise. It was said that aside from Chen Qingdu, no one was worth mentioning at the Sword Qi Great Wall. In the Wild Realm, aside from that gray-robed elder who could hold up the heavens, the rest were merely insignificant.

In this matter, neither sword immortals nor great demons had the right to mock the other.

Knowing that Yang Zhi had no intention of taking action, Huang Luan smiled and nodded, “This kid is persistently seeking death; I wonder how long he can remain lively.”

Huang Luan looked at Chen Ping'an, who was standing beside Lu Zhi. “It seems this brat holds a grudge against me. He probably blames me for interfering when he was fighting Li Zhen, sending him a ‘welcome gift.’ Now, he shifts the blame for his senior brother's serious injuries onto me. Such treatment, not only is he ungrateful, but he also has no sense of propriety. I think I should greet him.”

Huang Luan's thoughts stirred, and within the celestial city, an ancient palace with red walls and green tiles, fragrant incense wafting, vanished into thin air, along with a solitary mountain crowned with a stone tablet reading “Ancestral Thoughts of Autumn.” The mountain was barren, adorned only with withered trees, white grass, crimson leaves, and yellow flowers, exuding a sense of desolation and solemnity.

The ancient palace headed towards the city wall where Lu Zhi and Chen Ping'an stood, while the solitary mountain moved towards the two thatched cottages. The ancient palace was split in half by Lu Zhi’s sword strike, crashing heavily against the wall beneath them and turning into powder.

The Sword Immortal Wei Jin from the Snowstorm Temple appeared beside the stone tablet atop the solitary mountain. The next moment, countless sword lights erupted from every crack in the mountain’s flora and stones, then silently disappeared.

This man, the most talented cultivator in the Baoping Continent after Li Tuanjing of the Wind and Thunder Garden, had only just arrived at the Sword Qi Great Wall, still a Jade Purity Realm sword cultivator. In just a few years, after living in a small thatched cottage, he had participated in an offensive and defensive battle once and trained swordsmanship alongside the elder sword immortal and his neighboring peers, gaining a hint of the aura of an impending breakthrough to the realm of immortals.

Yang Zhi greeted Huang Luan, and before leaving, she cast a few more glances at the young man, imprinting his image in her mind.

Unexpectedly, the young man not only did not retreat but instead closed his folding fan and made a throat-cutting gesture, the slow movement strikingly conspicuous.

Huang Luan stifled a laugh, finding it amusing. Yang Zhi was the former master of the Yiluo River and a peak Ascendant Realm cultivator. If she were to act impulsively and earnestly compete with Chen Ping'an, it would definitely raise a commotion. Huang Luan would naturally welcome such a turn of events. The loss would fall upon Yang Zhi's subordinate forces, while the martial achievements would count towards Huang Luan's name. Even a mosquito's leg is meat. In the realm of righteousness, where everyone claimed their territory, the one with more elite troops would have a stronger foothold. It was all about human connections, seizing advantages, and seizing opportunities. This was no trivial matter.

However, Huang Luan refrained from speaking any inciting words, knowing it would backfire, making Yang Zhi more resolute and potentially harboring resentment towards her.

In the Wild Realm, there were no rules, which was quite comfortable, but it could also lead to trouble.

Yang Zhi smiled, “Huang Luan, if you can capture this brat and hand him over to me for punishment, apart from compensating you for your expenses, I can additionally offer you a sect's mountain gate from the righteous realm and even a capital city from a great dynasty. How about that?”

Huang Luan shook her head. “Before Chen Ping'an showed up today, I would have definitely agreed to this deal, but now, the price has gone down.”

Yang Zhi's expression darkened.

Huang Luan didn't even glance at the wild realm's female sovereign.

As Yang Zhi rode the wind away, she left behind a lingering phrase that echoed near Huang Luan's railing, “Don't regret it. Remember, if you dare to meddle with any dynasty's capital city beneath the mountains, you will be my enemy.”

Huang Luan rejected not only Chen Ping'an but also the alliance intention that Yang Zhi had implied.

Huang Luan was unfazed by Yang Zhi's threat.

The torrent of magical treasures formed by tens of thousands of demon practitioners remained impressively grand. However, compared to the orderly sword qi waterfall, the former appeared somewhat chaotic. 

Almost all sword immortals had begun to abandon the pursuit of personal gratification in their sword strikes. No longer was each strike a free and unrestrained expression of force; instead, nearly every sword released was imbued with utilitarian calculation. They needed to assess how to break through formations while also safeguarding their own Fifth Realm sword practitioners, and how to coordinate with sword immortals who were positioned far apart to jointly destroy critical treasures. They had to consider how to withdraw their swords while stealthily sending flying swords to either flank of the magical treasure torrent to decapitate some earth immortals among the demon practitioners.

Huang Luan naturally felt a pang of heartache but did not feel overly distressed. The real headache was the military tents in their own camp. 

Regarding their fourteen members' actions, the gray-robed elder had privately established a small rule: if bored, they could take a stroll near the city wall, but it was best not to exert themselves too much, especially with their core divine abilities and hidden techniques, which should ideally be reserved for the righteous realm.

The sword in Lu Zhi’s hand, a standard long sword from the sword workshop, could not withstand the impact of Lu Zhi’s sword intent and the collision with the ancient palace. After she sheathed the sword, it instantly shattered and vanished. She and Chen Ping'an stood on the city wall, turning to glance at the young man wielding the folding fan. “Does the Hidden Official intend to die so easily, or has he decided not to engage in the coming battles? I’m following the elder sword immortal’s orders to guard the formation. This is the duty of all sword practitioners of the Hidden Official lineage, not just Chen Ping'an. Think it through; don’t act impulsively.”

The nature of the great demons from the Wild Realm was nothing to discuss. Earlier, whether it was Chen Ping'an slaying Li Zhen or the two exchanging swords, those beasts did not feel anything was amiss because the Wild Realm never cared about major issues. Yet, for personal grudges, the higher the realm of the beasts, the clearer their memories. Thus, Chen Ping'an’s actions had directly forged deadly enemies with two great demons.

Chen Ping'an lightly tapped his head with the folding fan, and the female demon surprisingly held herself back, feeling some regret. Otherwise, Lu Zhi only needed to delay the great demon Yang Zhi for a moment, and three sword immortals who had already received word from the “Hidden Official” would take action: Yue Qing, Yuan Qingshu, and Wu Chengpei would each employ their own techniques and divine abilities to cut off her retreat. As for who would slay the great demon, it would certainly not be a single elder sword immortal but a multitude of sword immortals. Before reaching the city wall, Chen Ping'an had instructed Guo Zhujiu and Wang Xinshui that if any great demons approached the city wall, they should immediately send word to all the local sword immortals and encircle them.

Now at the Sword Qi Great Wall, even though it appeared that every sword immortal had their roles and worked in harmony to create the magnificent sword qi waterfall, once the Hidden Official's flying swords were dispatched, dozens of sword immortals would have to immediately redirect their sword tips. Even if it led to damage to the sword formations, all sword immortals would have to obey orders.

Chen Ping'an smiled and said, “When there are too many lice, they don’t itch; when there are too many debts, they don’t worry. It’s all about getting used to it. Huang Luan and Yang Zhi, once they act impulsively, might become a pair of desperate lovers instead of a celestial couple.”

There was one thing Chen Ping'an did not reveal: of the two flying swords from the “Hidden Official,” the more concealed one went directly to the elder sword immortal. Should any great demon approach, apart from the multitude of sword immortals making their moves, the elder sword immortal would also directly command Chen Xi and Qi Tingji to ensure the demon was slain. Under everyone’s watchful eyes, all sword immortals would intercept the intruder. The two hosts who had inscribed characters atop the city wall were merely opportunistic; no one would dare hold back.

Chen Ping'an not only concluded that the Hidden Official Xiao Xian was a traitor, but he also did not fully trust these two extremely lethal elder sword immortals. This initially appeared to be a significant misfortune.

In truth, it was a matter of trust, with measures in place for trusting. If distrust lingered, there would also be arrangements for that.

If Yang Zhi and Huang Luan believed that the current Sword Qi Great Wall was still the same as it had been for thousands of years, and thought they could traverse it safely, then they would have to pay a price. 

It wasn’t that the sword strikes of the Sword Qi Great Wall had not been high enough over the past ten thousand years. On the contrary, it was precisely because of the generosity and valor displayed by the sword immortals over the past ten thousand years that the sword cultivators of the Hidden Official lineage today had won the leeway to strategize.

Lu Zhi shook her head. “You’re thinking too simply. By the time you reach Yang Zhi’s age and realm, there aren’t many fools left.”

“I suppose I was too naive.” 

Chen Ping'an chuckled. “Fortunately, we haven’t suffered any losses.”

Lu Zhi waved her hand, “Hidden Official, please continue with your work; I’ll keep watch here.”

For this temporarily appointed Hidden Official, Lu Zhi felt she had done enough, even better than she had expected. However, if speaking purely of personal preferences, she held an average impression of Chen Ping'an. 

The reason was simple—he was ultimately not a sword immortal, nor even a sword cultivator.

Chen Ping'an jumped down from the city wall and returned to his desk. He smiled, “Looks like everyone is working hard for nothing. Since nothing came of it, it was merely a gamble for a slim chance.”

As he copied books, Chen Ping'an took the opportunity to review things for all the sword practitioners of the Hidden Official lineage, sharing more of his thoughts with his “subordinates.” He slowly continued, “In this siege by the Wild Realm, we have entered the third phase. The great demon Bai Ying was responsible for the first unveiling battle. Apart from changing the dynamics of time and location to some degree, it was more about reconnaissance and confirming the defensive details of the Sword Qi Great Wall. Coupled with some treacherous flying swords sent by traitorous sword practitioners, the Wild Realm gained an overwhelming advantage. This is an extremely delicate undertaking, which aligns closely with Bai Ying’s historical image. Among the fourteen great demons, Bai Ying has never favored brute force; she plays the game of wits. So if Bai Ying were stationed here, I wouldn’t even have to show up.”

Chen Ping'an paused, pondering briefly, then pointed to a location on a scroll depicting five mountain peaks, saying, “Next, Yang Zhi will be responsible for guarding the five mountain peaks on the battlefield. Compared to Bai Ying, who needs to constantly communicate with sixty military tents, Yang Zhi clearly doesn’t require many last-minute adjustments. Those five mountain peaks conceal five great demons, aiming to cut down our celestial realm sword practitioners. This strategy was set well in advance by the beasts and has little relation to Yang Zhi herself. Following her is the great demon Huang Luan. It’s clear that Yang Zhi is the most straightforward. Even in the face of the scheming between the Yiluo River and her deadly nemesis, the so-called strategies seem shallow. Thus, Yang Zhi is the one most likely to take action, even more so than Huang Luan. If it works out, regardless of whether Huang Luan or Yang Zhi dies at the city wall, as long as a peak great demon dies before the very eyes of all sword practitioners, it would be a tremendous gain for the Sword Qi Great Wall. The repercussions of Xiao Xian’s betrayal could be swiftly addressed by us new sword practitioners of the Hidden Official lineage.”

“What I’m betting on isn’t Yang Zhi’s lack of brains or her foolishness in not knowing the stakes; it’s her status as a scapegoat, betting on her lack of autonomy and on Huang Luan adding a little fuel to the fire. If the Sword Qi Great Wall cannot hold, and the demon clan invades the realm of righteousness, what do they seek? Naturally, it’s the countless miles of mountains and rivers, the great demons’ respective paths, and who do they seek? By relying on brute strength and military achievements? Of course, but the most crucial aspect is a word from the Moon Trampling Mountain, or more accurately, the heart’s intent of the great demon ancestors. It’s just a pity that Yang Zhi did not take the bait and was very cautious. This shows how practical the great demons of the Wild Realm are, which is something that I, along with all of you here, need to learn from. It’s also a reminder to our opponents, thus we cannot make assumptions.”

At this point, Chen Ping'an's gaze sharpened, repeating, “So we cannot make assumptions!”

Chen Ping'an immediately beamed with a smile, “Thus, for the upcoming fourth and fifth phases, whichever great demon is stationed, we can generally predict how the Wild Realm’s offensive will play out. Is it paced, understanding the art of war, or is it mindlessly rushing to death? We can actually make some predictions. However, the opposing side has a full sixty military tents, calculating even more meticulously than we do, making such predictions of limited significance, but better than nothing.”

On the southern city wall, Lu Zhi was left speechless. 

These words clearly stemmed from the Hidden Official’s previous observations atop the city wall. Feeling that there was no chance to converse further, it quickly turned into something she did not want to hear but had to.

Her impression of Chen Ping'an did not improve. 

However, Lu Zhi’s perception of the “Hidden Official” did unconsciously become a little better.

Gazing towards the southern battlefield, Lu Zhi then turned back to the “small world” where no one was striking. After turning back, she bore a hint of a smile.

Perhaps those sword practitioners were the kind of young people the elder sword immortal had been eagerly anticipating.

And she, Lu Zhi, along with many of today’s sword immortals, had likely once been such a young person.

Chen Ping'an looked at everyone, his expression sobering as he feigned shock, “At this point, you all still have no thoughts? I only know that if the Qi Refiners of the lower five realms keep striking, it will exhaust their spirit energy. I never knew that using your brains too much could make you duller.”

As the only sword cultivator of the Fifth Realm, Mi Yu was the most composed, not due to his high realm but because he felt that it had nothing to do with him. If the Hidden Official genuinely harbored discontent, it would be Lin Junbi, Xuan Can, and other younger, yet cunning and unscrupulous little rascals who would take the blame.

Deng Liang said solemnly, “The next army of demons forming the formation will all be sword practitioners. Our change in formation is essentially a lesson we’re teaching them how to wield swords. For example, how the sword immortals can exchange the cost of their strikes to maximize the overall lethality of the sword formation and how to concentrate the strikes of the top sword immortals to attempt to kill the enemy’s earth realm sword practitioners without warning will certainly be learned by them. Even if they only grasp the basic postures, in the next round of exchanges among sword practitioners, if we lack countermeasures, our losses will surely increase dramatically.”

Chen Ping'an pointed with his folding fan towards Lin Junbi, smiling, “Junbi, feel free to speak your mind.”

Lin Junbi immediately had his thoughts organized and smiled, “Given the current situation, we are at a disadvantage, and the sword formation naturally cannot be altered. However, we can change our approach and create a series of concealed traps surrounding all our key earth realm sword practitioners. From now on, all our sword immortals must take on an additional responsibility: to protect the formation of a certain earth realm sword practitioner. Furthermore, protecting the formation should not merely be about passive defense; that would be pointless. Every action must be aimed at fighting back, as we will no longer target the enemy’s earth realm sword practitioners but rather the enemy’s true top forces—the sword immortals!”

Chen Ping'an nodded.

Betting on that slim chance, if they couldn't slay Yang Zhi and Huang Luan, capturing several enemy sword immortals would also not be a loss.

Chen Ping'an had actually been waiting for Deng Liang and Lin Junbi to voice these thoughts. 

Once someone broke the ice, others quickly followed up with their ideas in the blink of an eye.

Gu Jianlong glanced at the confrontation between the flying swords and magical treasures on the scroll, then opened a book on the desk and nodded, “Then we need to quickly exhaust this reference text, striving to select ten to twenty of our earth realm sword practitioners as bait. This reference text was originally the responsibility of Wang Xinshui, and it’s clear that moving forward, it cannot still rest solely on his shoulders. Besides this, we can also conduct a training and evaluation for our sword immortals, trying out more possibilities. Previously, when sword immortals battled demons, they were too focused on individualism, usually just a few familiar sword immortal friends fighting side by side. However, this isn’t necessarily the best partnership. This reference text has become crucial for the next battle. This burden should not rest solely on Wang Xinshui.”

“Hidden Official, what do you think?”

Chen Ping'an propped his chin with one hand, his elbow on the desk, sitting sideways as if casually scribbling on a paper. Beside him lay the reference text already filled with several papers. Chen Ping'an kept writing, glanced at Gu Jianlong, and nodded with a smile, “Fair point. I’ll personally assist Wang Xinshui in perfecting the reference text, outlining the twenty earth realm sword practitioners who will serve as bait.”

Xuan Can followed Gu Jianlong’s train of thought, continuing, “Earlier, we had fewer opportunities to validate the pairing of our sword immortals’ strikes. This is a perfect opportunity to sharpen their skills, ensuring that the cooperation between sword immortals becomes increasingly smooth. With more tangible military achievements, the sword immortals won’t feel too stubborn. Otherwise, if our hidden lineage’s flying sword communications become stale over time, and the novelty fades, the sword immortals, with their lofty pride, will only become more reluctant to engage with us. So, the Hidden Official is correct; our enemies in the Hidden Official lineage, aside from those beasts from the Wild Realm, are our own sword immortals' realms, statuses, and sentiments! We must not overlook this! Regarding this matter, it cannot be a case of improvisation when we’re in a crisis. We need dedicated people to be responsible for this kind of research.”

Dong Buduo interjected, “Leave this to me.”

Lin Junbi hesitated for a moment.

Chen Ping'an said, “Dong Buduo will be responsible for the local sword immortals of the Sword Qi Great Wall, while Lin Junbi will handle all the foreign sword immortals. If Junbi has doubts, all the foreign sword practitioners, including Deng Liang, will answer any questions. As for certain private matters regarding senior sword immortals, should we keep them from the esteemed ones? Set aside those concerns for now. Even if the sword immortals become angry and resentful, it won't fall on your heads. I, this Hidden Official, am not afraid of bloodshed. If I can't protect your interests, then what kind of Hidden Official am I?”

Guo Zhujiu suddenly spoke, “What if the other party has already thought of the same answer as us, that surrounding and slaying the earth realm sword practitioners is a ruse, or even true, but inversely setting up an ambush for our sword immortals is even more real? What then?”

At this point, Guo Zhujiu looked worried as he turned to his master, the current Hidden Official.

Chen Ping'an chuckled, “Every step we take can only be counted as one or two steps behind. Can we win the game like this? I find it quite difficult. Thus, Guo Zhujiu’s concern is valid. We must always be more wary of the ‘what if’ than those beasts of the Wild Realm. They can withstand multiple contingencies, but we may only face one. If that happens, all the arrangements and efforts of our Hidden Official lineage will collapse and be rendered futile.”

Chen Ping'an turned to the relatively silent Pang Yuanji, “Pang Yuanji, think about how the great sword immortals in the A-volume standard text should adjust their positions atop the city wall and how they should collaborate their strikes. You can ponder that now. As per usual, the plans you come up with, I will take the blame for the bad ones.”

Pang Yuanji nodded, “No problem.”

Chen Ping'an spoke slowly, “According to the progress of the battle, within half a month at most, we will soon find ourselves in an extremely awkward position, where we feel like we’re unable to make ends meet. At that point, we will need to know every single sword practitioner of the Sword Qi Great Wall’s Fifth Realm and earth realm intimately. What then? Should we seek to learn more about the caves, sea-viewing realms, and dragon gate realms of the sword practitioners? We can learn, but that should not be the focus. The focus should be on the southern battlefield, in the A and B-volume primary and secondary texts, especially the thick C-volume that seems to have no last page.”

Chen Ping'an emphasized, “Everyone present, we sword practitioners of the Hidden Official lineage are destined to face disappointment, just varying in degree. Because none of us are perfect, everyone makes mistakes, and each of our small errors cannot be glossed over as mere mistakes. Once they occur, on the battlefield, they could lead to the disastrous consequence of thousands of casualties. All the hard-earned victories and the calculated advantages we’ve gained for the Sword Qi Great Wall can be forgotten by those who are supposed to be our allies. They may either come to scold us or remain silent yet resentful, but the most terrifying thing is silence—the silence of many.”

Feeling himself to be the most superfluous presence, Mi Yu could not help but speak, “Then let’s prove to them that they’re not wrong, but we’re even more right!”

Chen Ping'an opened his folding fan and fanned himself non-stop, “Who still dares to say that our Mi Yu sword immortal is superfluous? Who? Step forward, and I’ll spit in their face!”

Except for Mi Yu, who looked embarrassed, everyone else wore amused expressions.

Mi Yu, forcing a smile, said, “Thank you, Hidden Official.”

Chen Ping'an waved his hand, “Big Brother Mi is our Hidden Official’s anchor. No need for polite words; let’s keep it friendly!”

Gu Jianlong nodded, “Fair point!”

With Gu Jianlong, who was oblivious to the risks, leading the way, soon one after another, voices echoing the words of the Hidden Official arose.

“Agreed.”

“True.”

“Agreed.”

“No objections.”

Chen Ping'an closed the folding fan and lightly set it aside, “Let’s get to work and make some money!”

On the fan's surface, there were small characters written in tiny script. If one did not look closely, it appeared to be a blank fan surface.

Descending from the heavens, spring has arrived. The swords move down the mountain, and summer dares not approach.

A talisman boat docked at the northern city wall, and a person descended—dressed in a blue shirt and holding a sword, looking gaunt and exhausted, as if recovering from a serious illness. He stored the talisman boat into his sleeve and slowly walked toward the Hidden Official lineage.

Not only the sword practitioners of the Hidden Official lineage but even Mi Yu of the Jade Purity Realm was caught off guard.

The Hidden Official they had been with day and night was merely Chen Ping'an’s astral spirit venturing out?

It must be an illusion crafted by the elder sword immortal.

The astral spirit of Chen Ping'an smiled as he stood up, holding the folding fan. He stepped back, merging with the true body that walked forward.

Chen Ping'an lightly grasped the folding fan and walked to his seat, sitting cross-legged as he smiled, “I’ve missed you all.”

*(End of Chapter)*

 ### Chapter 740: Peril at Every Turn

The sword cultivators from the Hidden Official lineage were undeniable prodigies of the Dao, true paragons of talent. Their low cultivation levels could only be attributed to one reason: their youth. 

Thus, they were no strangers to the phenomenon of the Yin Spirit (Yin Shen) leaving the body for distant travels, although it was a rare occurrence among third-level Qi practitioners. Being able to remain detached from the physical realm for a prolonged period, unnoticed in the vast expanses filled with sword energy, was even more extraordinary. 

However, such oddities happening to Chen Ping'an didn't pique the curiosity of the sword cultivators, including Mi Yu. 

It was Lu Zhi who observed more keenly and directly asked through their mental connection, “Chen Ping'an, did you plan from the start to let Yang Zhi and Huang Luan take advantage of your earlier provocations?” 

While doodling in the third volume of the booklet, helping Wang Xinshui select twenty of their own Earth Immortal sword cultivators, Chen Ping'an replied with a ripple of his mind, “When ordinary fishing bait is cast into the water, it attracts big fish. Even if those big fish are finally dragged ashore, can the bait still remain? You yourself have said that a cunning old beast like Yang Zhi, having lived to his age, won't be foolish. The means to obstruct their retreat must naturally come from me first; otherwise, our sword immortal's ambush would be unsustainable.” 

Lu Zhi frowned, “Once the Yin Spirit collapses, it would damage the foundation of the Dao. As a Hidden Official, why must you go this far?” 

Chen Ping'an chuckled, “For the Yin Spirit of a third-level cultivator, trading it for one or two of the pinnacle ascendant beasts from the savage world is a bargain.” 

Lu Zhi hesitated momentarily; she did not appreciate Chen Ping'an's roundabout speech earlier, so she said bluntly, “Please be sincere with me.” 

After a brief silence, Chen Ping'an replied, “The Hidden Official lineage needs more than just invisible military achievements to establish itself. The biggest problem is that we remain behind the scenes, too comfortable. Everyone is a sword cultivator, yet no one has ever struck a single blow. This is fine during times of victory, but as casualties mount in the Sword Qi Great Wall, the Hidden Official lineage will inevitably face criticism. This is human nature. So, if I pay a little price early on, the whole Hidden Official lineage can avoid some mental strain. With the Hidden Official lineage clear-minded to strategize and deploy, in the long run, the benefits to the Sword Qi Great Wall will be immense.” 

Lu Zhi shook her head, “What you said is likely true, but I know you haven't revealed the full reason.” 

Chen Ping'an did not deny it. “Some thoughts must be kept close to the heart. Lu, the Great Sword Immortal, let’s not dig deeper into this; it’s meaningless.” 

For instance, why was he not devastated by the severe injuries to his senior brother? Was it merely because he was reserved and adept at hiding his feelings? Certainly not. 

Deep inside, Chen Ping'an hoped his senior brother would survive and live with a clear conscience; above all, he could never accept that “Zuo is dead.” 

The Great Sword Immortal once mentioned in the Ning residence's martial arts arena that if there was a good outcome, one should look back on life with kindness everywhere. 

It was in this vein that Chen Ping'an accepted that the Great Sword Immortal had confined his Yin Spirit and forbade him from sending word to his senior brother, urging him to be wary of a Hidden Official’s ambush. 

Afterward, when Chen Ping'an visited his senior brother at the thatched cottage, he felt no anger towards the Great Sword Immortal, nor did he hold any grudges. 

One should speak little of “what ifs” in life; after all, what if Zuo had been killed by the previous Hidden Official, Xiao Xun, with a single punch? 

Chen Ping'an concluded the conversation, “Lu Zhi, you focus on protecting the Hidden Official lineage with all your might. Just wield your sword; there’s no need to concern yourself with anything else.” 

Lu Zhi, rarely one for jokes, replied, “You carry yourself with such authority, Hidden Official.” 

Chen Ping'an could only awkwardly mimic his own disciples, pulling from the unorthodox teachings of Falling Star Mountain, and smiled as he added, “Your swordsmanship is divine, almost celestial. Whether my official stature is great in your eyes, I am but a laughingstock.” 

Lu Zhi laughed it off. 

Chen Ping'an was multitasking intensely. 

He sketched out various Earth Immortals in the third volume and communicated details with Wang Xinshui, who was in charge of the documentation. 

He paid close attention to the movements of the two scrolls along the horse path; this was the duty of a Hidden Official—delegation did not mean neglect. 

He also needed to observe the eleven sword cultivators closely, listening to their conversations and exchanges, much like a bureaucrat overseeing an inspection. 

Chen Ping'an set down his brush and habitually rubbed his wrist, unexpectedly reminded of Volume Six of “The Pearl Ship,” which mentioned “Young Wisdom.” 

Looking around, the eleven sword cultivators present, if they were in the Vast World (Haoran Tianxia), would likely qualify for both cultivation and scholarship given their talents. 

Among them, a few stood out particularly, like Xuan Can, who was practically a living map. His attention to and memory of the two scrolls surpassed even Chen Ping'an's capabilities. Xuan Can had a detailed account in his mind of every geographical feature on the battlefield, such as why a certain pit appeared, when it appeared, and how it would affect the ensuing combat; he had an exceptionally meticulous ledger in his mind. Others could achieve what Xuan Can did with effort, but it would require far more focus and would not come as naturally as it did to him. 

Thus, Chen Ping'an specifically requested Xuan Can to write a battlefield record, which would later serve as a reference for the other sword cultivators. 

Wang Xinshui had an astonishing instinct for predicting small-scale battles. Therefore, whenever Chen Ping'an found himself with some free time, he enjoyed observing Wang Xinshui, akin to taking a leisurely drink. 

When Wang Xinshui noticed the key moments on the scrolls where sword cultivators failed to strike perfectly or made too many mistakes, his expression would change; if the enemy's treasures coordinated too well, Wang Xinshui would become anxious. However, the battlefield was ever-changing, and to remember these details, Wang Xinshui often fixated on the scrolls, scribbling fervently, his handwriting almost illegible. Occasionally, he would appear dejected, seemingly unaware of whether what he saw, thought, remembered, or wrote would be useful, given that he, as a sword cultivator of the Hidden Official lineage, was too far from the battlefield. Could he replace the sword cultivators in battle? Thus, Wang Xinshui often displayed the most complex and vivid expressions; in just a few blinks, all emotions could cross his face, compounded by his habit of muttering to himself, making it all the more interesting. 

Lin Junbi’s overall planning skills resembled a kind of innate divine ability; as long as he had enough information and intelligence to support a battle, he rarely made mistakes. 

Guo Zhujiu was adept at envisioning worst-case scenarios—“unexpected events”—often thinking a step ahead, or even further. 

Thus, with Dong Budai and Lin Junbi collaborating on the book “The Sword Immortal’s Heart,” after Chen Ping'an had taken his seat, apart from clearly stating that Xuan Can would write a battlefield record, he also asked Wang Xinshui, Guo Zhujiu, and others to each write a “collection of essays.” Previously, Chen Ping'an had outlined twelve volumes, named after the heavenly stems, and now these could be named after the earthly branches. 

With both heavenly stems and earthly branches complete, the sword cultivators stood in the center, symbolizing harmony among people—a good omen, indeed. 

Dong Budai suddenly said, “What worries me is that the sword cultivators from the savage world might advance using the simplest method, focusing solely on their coordination, without considering anything else, and not seeking military achievements. If that’s the case, our subsequent calculations will all fall short. The most troubling part is that if we gain nothing, it’s a loss. If that happens, how shall we resolve it?” 

Chen Ping'an raised his head, chuckling softly, “It can be resolved. The battle at the Sword Qi Great Wall, with its grand strategies and heroic spirit, can become a double-edged sword; being immersed in battle, surrounded by familiar comrades who fall one after another, we mustn’t truly regard them as mere puppets devoid of education and emotions. After the thirteenth conflict, the demon clans’ assaults on the city were all practiced rehearsals; now the savage world has established sixty military camps. What does this imply? It means that every battlefield is under close scrutiny; the human heart is infectious.” 

“So, to prevent the enemy's sword formations from achieving a ‘stable but not losing’ state, we can take three actions: First, our sword formations should learn from the great hunts, mercilessly slaughtering the enemy troops. Second, for those we can’t kill, we should severely wound but not kill them; the more they suffer, the better. After withdrawing from the battlefield, these injured soldiers will become a natural source of resentment. Third, we should choose those who are bickering fiercely and love to quarrel, like the two seniors, Zhao Ge and Cheng Quan; I think they are quite suitable. While striking, they must curse the heavens and the earth, especially cursing the sword cultivators from the savage world, for their attempt to attack the city and seek out swords is essentially a ‘return to one’s roots.’ These words must be shouted by the sword immortals, especially the younger ones with louder voices, who should curse even more. If we accomplish these three tasks, we won’t allow the sword cultivators, whose lives are most valuable in the savage world, to think of doing anything extra; if the enemy is willing to act, we will have our chance.” 

At this point, Chen Ping'an laughed, “Earlier, when I faced Li Zhen in combat, did you truly believe I felt no hatred or anger at his words? How is that possible? At that moment, I could hardly wait to chew on his flesh, to flay that scoundrel. However, since it was merely a standoff, I couldn’t afford to be distracted for a moment and had to suppress that emotion. But afterward, when the two armies faced off, with tens of thousands of sword cultivators against tens of thousands of sword cultivators, the human heart always has some leeway. Remember, while we are focused on the two scrolls right before us, just beginning to understand the emotional threads of our sword immortals, we must also consider how the savage world perceives this war and all the battlefields. Once we understand this, many things could allow us to foresee the future, not only following the current but also creating our own momentum, turning it into a grand scheme where the savage world cannot enter.” 

Lin Junbi nodded, deeply moved, “Indeed, if our Hidden Official lineage could transform the entire battlefield into a small world, we could seize every advantage.” 

Chen Ping'an continued, “Imagine if we completely understood the thoughts of the Great Ancestor and the aspirations of the peak demon lords of the Fourteen Thrones? What kind of scene would that be?” 

Everyone fell silent in shock. 

Chen Ping'an chuckled, “Of course, this is impossible. Human power is limited; knowing when to accept fate is also a skill.” 

Guo Zhujiu suddenly said, “With a decent set of the second volume, I can actually follow the clues and delve into the hidden files of the previous Hidden Official lineage, gaining deeper insights into the secrets and undercurrents of the savage world. It might be worth guessing at the thoughts of those great demons. I certainly won’t waste time on trivial matters; you don’t need to worry one hundred percent, just one will suffice…” 

However, as soon as she uttered the title of ‘master,’ Guo Zhujiu immediately fell silent, irritated at her own slip of tongue. She felt guilty for embarrassing her master, as the rules of the Hidden Official lineage were still to be observed. 

Chen Ping'an replied, “It’s fine to call me master; just as I prefer it when others call me Chen Ping'an instead of addressing me awkwardly as 'Hidden Official.'” 

Gu Jianlong felt relieved and smiled brightly, but just as he was about to speak up, Chen Ping'an turned to him, saying, “Brother Gu, does this mean you've acknowledged your own ‘awkwardness’? You’re easily baited; you need to work on your heart. The Hidden Official’s courtesy is just that—courtesy. You really don’t need to stand on ceremony with me. If you were in the Vast World, relying solely on talent for your livelihood, you’d find it impossible to navigate the officialdom, literary circles, and the martial world.” 

Gu Jianlong looked as if he had lost his soul, fearing he might be subjected to some petty mischief. 

Chen Ping'an continued, “If it weren’t for Sword Immortal Mi providing that answer earlier, I might have regretted bringing up that topic. Everyone, we are here doing these things not because we must; even those foreign sword cultivators like Xuan Can, much less locals like Dong Budai and Pang Yuanzhi, should not bear the weight of heavy burdens alone. A careless misstep could shatter their Dao hearts. Compared to fighting on the city walls, which would you choose, Pang Yuanzhi?” 

Pang Yuanzhi replied honestly, “To strike.” 

Wang Xinshui was about to speak. 

Chen Ping'an smiled, “Hmm? Xinshui also has something to say?” 

Wang Xinshui quickly adapted, “Hidden Official, I want to second Pang Yuanzhi.” 

Wang Xinshui was indeed quite special; he was a genius sword cultivator whose thoughts moved swiftly, but his strikes often lagged behind. Because his cultivation was not high enough, he frequently hindered himself on the battlefield. It wouldn’t be accurate to say he acted recklessly; every suggestion he made was quite apt. However, Wang Xinshui himself could not express himself with swordplay, nor could his friends. Hence, he earned the title of one of the recent five prodigies of the Sword Qi Great Wall: “I can prepare before the battle, but afterward, it’s all mine.” 

Fortunately, there hadn’t been overly severe casualties. However, Wang Xinshui felt very conflicted about the idea of participating in battle—not out of fear of death but because it left him feeling restless, as if he was constantly bumping against his own heart’s desires. 

Chen Ping'an chuckled, “We’ve exchanged enough pleasantries. From now on, I may frequently leave this place and roam around. If you harbor resentment, remember to hide it well. Moreover, when it comes to going out to fight, you certainly won’t have the chance; I will, so just envy me.” 

The composed yet flexible Deng Liang spoke up, “A golden child does not sit in a cluttered hall. This may be a huge joke in the Sword Qi Great Wall, but here, Hidden Official, you should still think twice before acting. Even if you truly want to leave the city walls to fight, please be cautious of your whereabouts. Without you, our Hidden Official lineage would be forced to change commanders at the front line, which is a great military taboo.” 

“Thank you for your kind intentions. This kind of frankness should be a rule of our Hidden Official lineage. Behind closed doors, we are all family; family should speak a few harsh words to each other, and that is a good thing.” 

Chen Ping'an added, “However, those who can kill me, like Yang Zhi and Huang Luan, still dare not take risks to act. As for the other beasts, they’re forgetful and disbelieving in evil; they can certainly come find me to test their luck.” 

Deng Liang recalled the earlier moment when the female sword immortal Xie Songhua achieved her victory with a single strike and kept silent thereafter. 

Chen Ping'an stood up, “I’m going to find my two seniors, Nalan Shao Wei and Yan Ming, for a chat.” 

He grabbed the “Hidden Official” jade token and hung it at his waist. He needed to discuss the matters regarding the cross-continental ferry at the Upside-Down Mountain with these two fellow travelers. This wasn’t something that could be clarified in a few words; it required a face-to-face meeting. 

Some matters could only be addressed in the capacity of the Hidden Official. 

Walking along the horse path, Chen Ping'an muttered to himself, “In the world of knowledge, nothing is more difficult to deal with than a night sailing ship.” 

Mi Yu glanced at the young man’s back, feeling a strange swirl of unexplainable emotions. 

Earlier, Chen Ping'an's distant travels with his Yin Spirit stationed at the Hidden Official lineage had been peculiar. 

His words and actions always carried a sense of danger and strangeness, each sentence deeply thoughtful, accumulating authority invisibly, tightening the grip on the Hidden Official’s power, even leading people to unconsciously ponder Chen Ping'an’s thoughts. 

Now, however, Chen Ping'an seemed to have shifted his mindset. 

Which was better, Mi Yu couldn’t say. 

In truth, it was all just a mess. 

He was, after all, a Jade Purity Realm sword cultivator, yet here he found himself as the most reticent one, especially as he thought of his grievances with the Wen Sheng lineage, which only added to his frustration. 

In the end, Mi Yu rubbed his chin, muttering, “Is my mind really that dull?” 

Suddenly, Chen Ping'an turned and called out, “Sword Immortal Mi, join me; I estimate you will soon have your hands full.” 

With no choice but to follow along, Mi Yu felt a sense of relief after speaking with Chen Ping'an, realizing it was a good thing; he could also take a breather at the Upside-Down Mountain. 

Not only that, but Chen Ping'an even actively asked Mi Yu for his thoughts on whether certain ideas were feasible. 

Mi Yu spoke honestly, refuting one by one. 

This young Hidden Official didn’t seem to be particularly disheartened. 

The owner of the Spring Fan Pavilion, Shao Yunyan, was well-known for being reclusive at the Upside-Down Mountain. 

Today, Shao Yunyan had strolled through the four major private residences, passing by the Ape Ruan Mansion, the Water Crystal Palace, and the Plum Blossom Garden, merely glancing at them from a distance. 

Having cast an illusion spell and not being one to seek the limelight, very few recognized this sword immortal. 

Finally, Shao Yunyan found a tavern, knocked on the door with his magic, and the ripples spread out. The door opened, and he stepped over the threshold. Inside, the business remained dismal; aside from himself, there were no other customers. 

In this dwindling paradise, he aimed to drink a cup of Forgetting Worries Wine. 

It was almost a ritual for every wandering sage who traveled to the Upside-Down Mountain. 

The old man sat behind the counter, dozing off, while on the counter sat a jade poem of an eight-treasure birdcage, where a small yellow sparrow dozed just like the old man. 

A young man named Xu Jia spotted Shao Yunyan and was quite pleased, primarily because he remembered the owner of the Spring Fan Pavilion had once borrowed a gourd vine from him. Thus, among the many familiar patrons, Xu Jia, known for his laziness, was especially attentive today, quickly bringing a jar of wine to the table. 

Although Xu Jia had never interacted with Shao Yunyan, he had heard that this sword immortal from the Northern Julu Continent had visited here long ago, drinking wine, but unable to pay, he had traded a sword-raising gourd from the gourd vine for a jar of wine and ended up drunkenly intoxicated. Later, after making money, he regretted not paying the market price, offering a bunch of Gu Yu coins instead, but the tavern owner refused, and Shao Yunyan, somewhat offended, never returned to drink. 

Standing against the wall, Shao Yunyan looked around and smiled, “It’s been seven or eight hundred years since I last came, and it’s almost covered a wall. Is the business here that good?” 

Xu Jia complained, “The people are infuriating. I heard there’s a tavern at the Sword Qi Great Wall selling that terrible wine, which just opened over a year ago, and their useless signboards are almost covering three walls now.” 

Shao Yunyan apologized to the young waiter, picked up the jar of Forgetting Worries Wine, and sat back at the table where he first drank all those years ago. He poured himself a bowl of wine and looked toward the counter, saying with a smile, “Shopkeeper, that gourd vine has already been taken by a young girl to the Water Scripture Mountain in the Northern Julu Continent. In about a decade or so, that gourd for raising swords will be ripe, and I’ll trouble you to send someone to retrieve it. Regarding the ownership of this gourd, I’ve already informed Water Scripture Mountain; the person will show up to take it, it’s that simple.” 

The old man grunted and opened his eyes, glancing at Xu Jia, “Are you going?” 

Xu Jia asked, “If I leave the tavern and just happen to have the young lady return, what should I do?” 

The old man laughed and scolded, “I just don’t understand, why do you have to hang yourself from one tree? My daughter has no beauty, no figure, and her mind is muddled; she’s been attached to someone for a long time. How could she possibly be worthy of you?” 

Xu Jia retorted, “I’ve been here since childhood; how many girls have I seen? If I don’t like the young lady, who else would I like?! Would I like you, old man?” 

The old man wasn’t angry. His daughter had been away for many years, and with only the old man and the young one remaining in this desolate place, he couldn’t afford to scold him. If he were too harsh, there would be a risk of his daughter running away again, leading to significant losses for the tavern. 

The old man smiled, “Then you should get out of here and go see the world; the truly beautiful women will dazzle you.” 

Xu Jia nodded, “I also miss Cao Ci. Once I get that sword-raising gourd in the Northern Julu Continent, I’ll go find him in the Central Continent.” 

At this point, Xu Jia walked over to the counter, shaking the birdcage, and scolded, “You fool, why couldn’t you recognize Chen Ping'an’s martial roots back then? Did you think it was all just a sham?” 

The yellow sparrow in the cage was of the same breed as the yellow sparrow of the three palm sects of Qingtian, yet one was to test literary fortune, while the other tested martial fortune. 

Shao Yunyan chuckled, “Shopkeeper, got a story to tell?” 

The old man waved his hand, “Just drink your wine. Treating Forgetting Worries Wine as ordinary wine is a waste. If it weren’t for that sword-raising gourd, I wouldn’t care to sell you a drop of wine.” 

As Shao Yunyan drank, he casually asked, “Is the Water Crystal Palace still dreaming of making a fortune, thinking only of profits? They can’t seem to change, but the Ape Ruan Mansion has already cleared out. Still, none of that matters; I just want to know where this tavern will be located in the future. There are countless types of celestial wines, and I’ve practically drunk them all. The only ones I still remember fondly are your Forgetting Worries Wine and the Qing Shen Mountain wine from the Bamboo Sea Cave.” 

The old man glanced at his disciple, still sulking with the yellow sparrow, and bypassed the counter to bring a jar of wine, sitting down beside Shao Yunyan and pouring a bowl for each to enjoy. 

The old man said, “I’m an outsider, and you’re an outsider; naturally, you’re more comfortable. Why meddle in these affairs? Since you’ve meddled, whether this tavern opens here or in the far reaches of the sky, even if you find the answer, can you still drink the wine?” 

Shao Yunyan laughed and asked, “Can I speak my mind?” 

The old man nodded, “You know the rules of the tavern. The drunken words of the drinkers will not go outside.” 

Shao Yunyan looked toward the tavern's entrance, where white mist swirled, and softly said, “Years ago, I promised the Sword Qi Great Wall to do something; I can’t back out.” 

The old man asked, “Can’t you run?” 

The old man quickly nodded, “Difficult.” 

Shao Yunyan laughed, “No need to run. As long as you don’t leave the Upside-Down Mountain in a grand manner and act a bit sneaky, it’ll be fine.” 

The old man paused for a moment, “In that case, are you still willing to stay? With your level of cultivation and swordsmanship, it’s not enough to be of use; you’re just courting death. It’s better to die drunk than to die foolishly. Fine, I’ll give you another jar of wine.” 

Shao Yunyan said, “The Hidden Official has already defected to the savage world.” 

The old man raised an eyebrow, “That Xiao Xun girl holds such great resentment against the Vast World?” 

Shao Yunyan laughed, “I heard a new Hidden Official has taken charge. If you can guess who it is, I won’t drink a jar of wine from your tavern for free; you can take three guesses.” 

The old man pondered for a moment, “Is it the one who made the most money following Ah Liang, or is it that girl Ning Yao? It wouldn’t be that child chosen by Xiao Xun, would it? What was his name again?” 

Xu Jia replied, “I believe it’s Pang Yuanzhi.” 

Shao Yunyan burst into laughter, “A jar of Forgetting Worries Wine for free; my spirits are high.” 

Shao Yunyan drank two jars of Forgetting Worries Wine in one go and, feeling tipsy, left the tavern, satisfied with his visit. 

The old tavernkeeper shared some amusing tales with him, such as inner secrets concerning the fifth realm of the world. The vast rivers and mountains stretched for thousands of miles, containing treasures of geomancy and ancient sites, new paradises waiting to be claimed. It seemed the Qingtian realm could also share in the fortune, with various astonishing pathways of the Dao awaiting those fated to encounter them. The old tavernkeeper imparted the most weighty gossip, something Shao Yunyan had never heard of or even imagined: many Confucian saints, not only establishing their territories and stabilizing the world throughout the ages, had quietly fallen in battle, and the number of those who died in war was not small. Thankfully, the “Sage of Rites,” who was said to be “transcending the earthly realm,” was still present, leading Confucian saints into the unknown beyond the heavens, standing against some obstinate ancient deities for a long time. 

Shao Yunyan couldn’t help but ask a question at that moment, “Is it unnecessary for the other three realms?” 

The old tavernkeeper shook his head, “Unnecessary.” 

Shao Yunyan wanted to ask the reason behind that. 

As the ancestor of a hundred schools of thought, the old man said, “Not knowing is for the best.” 

Shao Yunyan strolled back through a scene much like the Ape Ruan Mansion, returning to his own residence. 

Every step he took was fraught with peril. 

Because they were all atop the Upside-Down Mountain. 

Traveling with Sword Immortals Ku Xia and Lin Junbi along the border of the Sword Qi Great Wall, they neither remained at the city walls to slay enemies nor followed young men like Jiang Guancheng to Nan Posa Continent. 

Sitting in that Plum Blossom Garden, he played chess with the rosy-faced lady, basking in the romance of life. 

Yet today, he left the garden and went to the Ferry Pavilion to observe the back-and-forth of the cross-continental ferries. 

The Ferry Pavilion was regarded as the most misnamed scenic spot at the Upside-Down Mountain, yet it remained bustling every day; the small pavilion was always packed with people except during the deep of night. 

Bian Jing didn’t join the crowd but sat on a white jade viewing platform railing outside the Ferry Pavilion, speaking to himself through mental waves. 

Bian Jing chuckled, “Aren’t you always boasting about being old friends with that old deaf man? There are no other sword immortals guarding the prison where the old deaf man is; there’s no chance at all for anything to happen?” 

“Not a chance; it’s best not to touch that mess.” 

Bian Jing sighed, “I just can’t understand how you savage world beings, with such high cultivation, can still be so narrow-minded.” 

“Using crafty tricks, twisting and turning, is that also a part of the Dao?” 

Bian Jing, ever the instigator, smiled and asked, “Is that ‘Dao Old Two’ who caused your downfall really invincible?” 

“Without truly facing him, you wouldn’t grasp the terror of that rotten old bull’s nose.” 

Bian Jing expressed regret, “It’s a pity that Lady Gui from the Old Dragon City in Baopingzhou didn’t agree to Lady Hongyan's invitation.” 

“It’s a pity; her true form is the most orthodox Moon Palace type. If she were willing to collaborate on a grand scheme, our odds would be even greater.” 

Bian Jing laughed, “We? It’s you who should say that; I'm just a little role with no say.” 

“Even if I’m a little role, my heart still belongs to me; don’t act like an innocent bystander.” 

Bian Jing remarked, “According to the latest news from Lady Hongyan, many sword immortals with stirring hearts are currently in a very awkward position, practically sitting on a wax figure. They probably can’t wait to hack that second shopkeeper to pieces.” 

This time, the “old immortal” didn’t engage with Bian Jing. 

Bian Jing gazed at the cross-continental ferries, noticing the joy on everyone’s faces that was hard to conceal, and he smiled, “Seeing so many people like this lifts my spirits significantly; I no longer feel guilty.” 

Coming to the Upside-Down Mountain to conduct business with the Sword Qi Great Wall, trading items for items, was the most profitable endeavor—arriving laden and returning even more heavily laden. Once back in their home continent, they could flip their goods for staggering profits. 

“Three years without opening, when we do, we feast for three years,” this was about those ferries conducting various businesses. 

Moreover, during times of great war, every round trip of these ferries became increasingly profitable, as they held the bargaining chips for rock-bottom pricing. 

Bian Jing nodded, “There’s no right or wrong; only positions. A profound truth, I wholeheartedly agree.” 

A ripple of mental waves arose, “Is that sarcasm?” 

Bian Jing laughed and shook his head, “No, I genuinely feel that way. Just like having a fist is the only truth; I completely endorse that.” 

Bian Jing surveyed his surroundings. 

Soon, the world would change. 

(End of Chapter)

 ### Chapter 741: Assassination of the Hidden Official

Chen Ping'an first found Yan Ming, and the two strolled together, with Mi Yu following at a distance.

One was trying to retrieve the Yan family's account books, while the other was inquiring in detail about the trading rules concerning the Sword Qi Great Wall and the cross-continental ferry to the Upside-Down Mountain. 

The real issue at hand was the Yan family's financial situation. If they fronted some divine money, how long could they afford to sustain losses in a series of transactions, and how could the Sword Qi Great Wall compensate for the Yan family's losses?

One was a small sect, and the other a wealthy merchant; the two conversed for over half an hour, each calculating their own interests.

On the way, Chen Ping'an spoke openly with Mi Yu. Mi Yu felt that it was difficult to discuss matters with Nalan Shaowei, but with Yan Ming, there should be no significant issues. After all, Chen Ping'an was already a Hidden Official and had been given a great authority in times of crisis. Furthermore, Chen Ping'an and the Yan family's eldest son had a very good relationship, so Yan Ming should be willing to help him out, both for public and private reasons. Most importantly, Chen Ping'an's words held weight with the Grand Sword Immortal.

After bidding farewell to Yan Ming, Chen Ping'an went to find Nalan Shaowei. In terms of external commerce, both the Yan family and the Nalan family were prestigious names associated with the Sword Qi Great Wall. The top three families—Dong, Chen, and Qi—controlled the clothing, sword-making, and alchemy industries, making Yan Ming and Nalan Shaowei true financial deities in a sense.

Mi Yu asked, "Was it smooth sailing?"

Chen Ping'an chuckled self-deprecatingly, "The general direction is fine, but there are many stumbling blocks with the details. I thought I could start easy with the two seniors and then tackle the hard stuff, but it seems it's going to be harder than I thought."

Mi Yu teased, "Those times when the Hidden Official called him 'Uncle Yan' must have been for nothing."

Immediately, this sword immortal, who loved to drink and enjoy the moon, showed a hint of irritation. "Is Yan Ming too ungrateful? Not giving an ounce of respect to the Hidden Official? I’ve got the logic down—unity in glory and loss—but Yan Ming is being so indecisive. Did he not want to climb the city after losing both arms in his youth, or is he just afraid that the Hidden Official will take his financial power?"

Mi Yu was not the least bit intimidated by Yan Ming, who had fallen from the Golden Core realm.

There was an abundance of divine money, yet it couldn't be used on his life-protecting flying sword. This pitiful situation was worse than those sword cultivators who diligently fought monsters and painstakingly nurtured their swords.

Chen Ping'an shook his head, saying, "It’s not that simple. Yan Ming is very meticulous with his accounts. Since the general direction has been agreed upon, it’s not a bad thing to negotiate the details further. I can just meet him a few more times. That being said, Yan Ming's attitude shows he doesn't think the Hidden Official is worth more than divine money, which is a true responsibility to the Sword Qi Great Wall."

Mi Yu quietly asked, "Hidden Official, do you truly harbor no grievances?"

Chen Ping'an replied, "More often, it’s about enjoying the comfortable things. For someone like Mi Jianxian, such an extraordinary being, it’s quite difficult to advance boldly in their realm. Tough times are to be endured; every bit of it is beneficial."

Mi Yu fell silent.

There was still some resentment. However, he had no means to deal with Yan Ming, so he pitied himself instead.

Yet, Mi Yu could tolerate the direct words from Chen Ping'an; what truly bothered him were the polite smiles from certain sword immortals, who greeted him merely as a courtesy. For instance, the past Li Tui, or those who didn’t even bother to glance at him, like the grand sword immortal Yue Qing, who shared a close bond with his brother Mi Hu. With Mi Yu, Yue Qing never spoke ill words because he simply wouldn’t speak at all. Those dull blades, wrapped in silk, were the most damaging to a sword heart.

Chen Ping'an laughed, "Let’s keep the harsh words between ourselves, Mi Jianxian."

Upon arriving at Nalan Shaowei's place, the old sword immortal merely stated, "I never concern myself with financial matters; go speak with Nalan Caihuan."

Chen Ping'an then sought out Nalan Caihuan, a female sword cultivator of the Golden Core realm. While her level wasn't high, she was adept at managing her household and generating wealth.

At this, Mi Yu truly lost his temper. "This old Nalan is being too unreasonable?!"

Chen Ping'an remained silent.

Mi Yu only dared to grumble after the fact.

Earlier, he had been too intimidated to even breathe in front of Nalan Shaowei.

They found Nalan Caihuan, a beautifully adorned woman with a graceful figure. Her hair was pinned up with a jade hairpin, its tail intricately carved into a lifelike dragonfly. She had delicate features with dark eyebrows, wearing a thin silk gown with golden threads, and stepping into a pair of red brocade shoes, she was recognized as a great beauty in the Sword Qi Great Wall.

She looked like a pampered noblewoman, yet when she reached the battlefield, her sword was as fierce and sharp as Qi Shou. 

Mi Yu felt conflicted and purposely wore a cold expression.

Nalan Caihuan and Mi Yu were peers, and although Mi Yu was regarded as a decorative pillow in the eyes of sword immortals, many women admired him, and those who desired him often cursed him more fiercely than men. Nalan Caihuan was one of them. Before Mi Yu became a sword immortal, his life had been too smooth, which led to his saying, "Affection has never endured through the ages." In reality, it wasn't that he couldn't hold onto anyone, but rather that the devoted women from the Sword Qi Great Wall and the world of Haoran simply couldn't hold onto him.

Mi Yu observed people.

What Chen Ping'an saw, however, were the mountains of gold and silver belonging to the Nalan family.

The first words that Chen Ping'an spoke almost made Mi Yu lose his composure.

"Nalan Madam, your family head has agreed to assist me. The old sword immortal is deeply principled and sacrifices his family's interests to help the Sword Qi Great Wall through this crisis. However, he also reminded me that the Nalan family is under your authority, so I should inform you."

After that, Nalan Caihuan collected her thoughts and began discussing the subsequent arrangements and negotiating details with the Hidden Official who had received the "ancestor's decree."

The two returned along the path leading back to the Hidden Official's area.

Mi Yu found it absurd and softly asked, "When Nalan Caihuan chats with Nalan Shaowei later, won’t the Hidden Official’s cover be blown?"

Chen Ping'an replied, "Sky-high prices, pay based on ability. If Nalan Shaowei doesn’t want to hear what I say, then let Nalan Caihuan speak on it."

Finally, Chen Ping'an joked, "If Nalan Madam comes to accuse me, I reckon that Mi Jianxian alone can handle her. But if Nalan Shaowei personally comes to attack me, you, Big Brother Mi, must protect me."

Mi Yu forced a smile, "Isn’t there still Lu Zhi? It's not up to me to wrestle with that old Nalan."

Whether it was Nalan Shaowei or Lu Zhi, they both ranked among the top ten sword immortals of the Sword Qi Great Wall, and in the past, even if Mi Yu didn’t take a detour upon seeing them, he would still feel ashamed and filled with awe.

Most of the friends Mi Yu could converse with were sword cultivators at the Fifth Level, and many were flirts; there were very few sword immortals at the Sixth Level.

As he accompanied Chen Ping'an, only one sword immortal of the jade purity realm called out to Mi Yu, named Lie Ji. In terms of cultivation, he was a kindred spirit with Mi Yu, belonging to the category of those who were outstanding in youth but ultimately fell short. In the world of Haoran, it might be a significant regret unique to sword immortals, yet in the Sword Qi Great Wall, it was an open joke.

It was said that Lie Ji was impatient with quietude and was quite talkative, once having the nickname "Magpie." However, the young people of the Sword Qi Great Wall didn’t find such a ridiculous nickname fitting for Sword Immortal Lie Ji.

Lie Ji often came to find Mi Yu to drink and relieve his boredom.

At this moment, when Lie Ji saw Chen Ping'an, he cheerfully called out, "Hidden Official!"

Chen Ping'an, originally strolling with his sleeves draped, smiled and nodded, extending his hand from his sleeve, clasping his fists in return.

After walking a distance, Chen Ping'an joked, "Mi Jianxian has a wide circle of friends! I’m fortunate to benefit from that."

Mi Yu glanced at the southern wall, and like Pang Yuanji, he actually preferred to draw his sword and slay monsters.

In the following days, apart from overseeing the Hidden Official’s area, Chen Ping'an frequently summoned Mi Yu to discuss matters with important figures.

All of them were big shots.

For instance, the sages of the Confucian and Buddhist sects located at both ends of the Sword Qi Great Wall.

Chen Ping'an wanted to clarify the ins and outs regarding the "Dispute of Heavenly Timing."

During this time, Mi Yu noticed that Ning Yao had donned a robe of celestial-grade quality, along with a newly crafted sword box containing two long swords. One of those swords was the very one Chen Ping'an used to slay Li Zhen, aptly named "Sword Immortal." It was indeed a fine name. No wonder the young Hidden Official occasionally chatted idly with Gu Jianlong and Wang Xinshui at the desk, claiming that he had exceptional talent in naming things; if naming were the only great path to cultivation in the world, he would already be at the threshold of immortality.

Pang Yuanji casually mentioned that the Hidden Official’s line had collected thousands of years' worth of archived records. The summer retreat and winter residence had been properly categorized and were numerous. It was impossible to move them all to the horse-walking path for searching and perusing, making it much more convenient to browse through them there, especially at the summer retreat, which was of utmost importance. Rather than waiting until the last minute and making someone run back and forth, it would be better to just move the necessary archives to the summer retreat. The Hidden Official’s message-carrying flying swords were indeed rapid; they could simply transfer one of the scrolls to one of the residences. Otherwise, with all the sword cultivators from the Hidden Official’s line gathered at the horse-walking path, they would surely attract the attention of great monsters. Remaining atop the city walls meant they were already sacrificing the combat power of the great sword immortal Lu Zhi.

Almost every sword cultivator from the Hidden Official’s line agreed and supported Pang Yuanji’s proposal.

Only Chen Ping'an did not consent, stating that there was no rush for now, and he had his own plans regarding when to move to the summer retreat.

In this matter, neither Dong Budu nor Deng Liang had any intention of continuing the debate. Both held differing opinions on the Hidden Official’s decision, voicing their dissent one after another.

Dong Budu emphasized that the Hidden Official’s line was too important, and staying on the horse-walking path risked being wiped out in one fell swoop.

Deng Liang lamented even more about the great sword immortal Lu Zhi remaining stationed there, which completely contradicted the Hidden Official’s line's principle of meticulousness and relentless pursuit.

Guo Zhujiu, unusually silent, lowered her head, wishing she could stare holes into the books and desks, her heart heavy.

And the girl’s silence itself was a form of attitude.

For Guo Zhujiu, who held the highest status in the world of her master, this was still an unprecedented action.

Yet Chen Ping'an still did not agree, providing additional reasons, but unable to truly convince everyone. Thus, the overall atmosphere among the sword cultivators of the Hidden Official’s line grew somewhat serious.

Afterward, the great sword immortal Yue Qing took the time to visit, halting at the edges of the sword qi barrier drawn by Mi Yu before continuing on.

Chen Ping'an immediately stood up and approached Yue Qing.

The two did not approach the other sword cultivators of the Hidden Official's line.

Yue Qing smiled and said, "Chen Ping'an, you need not worry about my face. I came this time not just to apologize to the disciples of the Confucian Sage but also to express my thanks to you—who is not just the Hidden Official."

Chen Ping'an nodded, "No need to stand on ceremony, I accept."

Yue Qing continued, "I previously criticized you regarding the Confucian Sage, and I did not hold back. Now that I’m here to apologize, naturally it feels a bit awkward. To be honest, if it were someone else in your position as the Hidden Official, no one would have dared to concern themselves with how I wield my sword. I would not be so polite."

Chen Ping'an replied, "As a candidate for the top ten sword immortals, you should have such boldness."

Yue Qing rubbed his chin and said, "You indeed handle matters decisively. I recognize that, but your way of speaking is truly not appealing to me."

Chen Ping'an passed a jug of wine to him.

Yue Qing laughed heartily, accepting the jug and leaving on his sword.

Chen Ping'an looked up, not withdrawing his gaze for a long time.

This was how a great sword immortal should be—standing firm on the bottom line, clear on likes and dislikes.

Returning to his seat, just as he sat down, Guo Jianlong said with a smile, "Hidden Official, don’t be stingy. You gave a jug of wine to Great Sword Immortal Yue; we, your own people, should not be treated any worse, right?"

Cao Jun laughed, "The wine in the jar is freshly brewed, truly invigorating."

Xuan Shen then chimed in, "I have yet to taste the immortal brew from the wine shop; it’s a regret in life. I hope to remedy that."

Guo Zhujiu slammed her palm on the table, "Pay up first!"

Chen Ping'an smiled, "There is indeed wine, but we can discuss that later. After killing a few earth immortal sword cultivators from the wild world, I’ll bring out a few jars of wine to celebrate."

The room erupted in noise.

Guo Jianlong and Wang Xinshui were the most enthusiastic.

Dong Budu did not even raise his head, clicking his tongue, "You’re quite bold."

Immediately, Guo Jianlong turned to Wang Xinshui, saying, "Xinshui, what’s wrong with you?"

Wang Xinshui looked innocent, "I’m just learning from you."

After this round of banter, the previously heavy atmosphere lightened somewhat.

Today, Chen Ping'an again rose to leave, walking to another part of the city wall.

Mi Yu had resigned himself, now finding himself a part of two more jokes, becoming the highest-ranked sword cultivator in the Hidden Official’s line, and then turning into the sycophantic follower of the young Hidden Official.

As he walked along, half-baked sword immortals would joke, "With Mi Brother here, why would we need Great Sword Immortal Lu to protect the Hidden Official's line?"

There were even insinuations that poked fun at the Hidden Official himself, "Mi Jianxian, you’re so free, just enjoying the scenery?"

Mi Yu looked at Chen Ping'an, who always wore a cheerful expression, wondering if this was what they called "spitting on one’s face and drying it off?"

Some of Guo Jianlong's fair comments were indeed fair and hit the nail on the head.

Once again, they passed by Lie Ji.

In between sheathing his sword and sipping wine, Lie Ji stood up upon seeing the two pass near the wall, taking out two jugs of wine from his belongings and tossing them to Mi Yu and Chen Ping'an, saying, "This is from the second shopkeeper."

Mi Yu caught the jug, which contained a snowflake money bamboo sea cave wine. Lie Ji was truly stingy even when flattering.

Chen Ping'an also reached out to catch the jug of bamboo sea cave wine.

In an instant.

An anomaly occurred.

A fierce red sword light suddenly shot out, the density of sword qi made the sword light appear almost dripping with vivid color.

It turned out to be Lie Ji's life-protecting flying sword "Burning Flower," aimed directly at the heart of the new Hidden Official, Chen Ping'an.

Mi Yu's heart was in turmoil; he directly crushed the wine jug and instantly summoned his life-protecting flying sword "Sky Full of Haze" to try to block Lie Ji’s flying sword.

Even if he couldn't completely stop it, he had to buy Chen Ping'an a chance to respond. No matter how heavy the injury, it was better than being pierced through the heart by Lie Ji’s direct attack. A sword immortal’s flying sword, aside from harming someone, would leave sword qi lingering in the enemy's acupoints, which was an immense trouble. 

Though Lie Ji and Mi Yu might be looked down upon by other sword immortals, Lie Ji's strike was imminent, and Chen Ping'an was completely defenseless, reaching out to accept that potentially lethal jug of wine. Mi Yu could only pray for Chen Ping'an's survival!

Mi Yu's life-protecting flying sword "Sky Full of Haze," even if it was slightly late, still managed to bump against the tail of "Burning Flower," causing the latter’s tip to deviate slightly from its aim at Chen Ping'an’s heart.

At the same time, Mi Yu stepped forward, drawing his sword as he rushed toward the flying sword that Lie Ji had launched.

Mi Yu’s sword was of extremely high quality, due to the gifts from his brother Mi Hu, while Lie Ji had neither a partner nor a teacher, his sword was merely an ordinary length sword from a sword shop.

After being slightly deflected by Mi Yu’s flying sword, Lie Ji's "Burning Flower" still charged ahead.

Chen Ping'an formed hand seals. Without the protection of his celestial-grade robe, he was now wearing a blue robe from the Ning family, along with a standard robe from the clothing shop. Especially the inner robe, which glimmered with precious light and rippled as it finally coalesced into a faint golden talisman—the Sword Lock Talisman.

However, the distance between Lie Ji and Chen Ping'an was simply too close, and with Lie Ji unleashing his life-protecting sword without holding anything back, the flying sword surged forth relentlessly.
