The old master, who was the Great Heaven Monarch’s first disciple, was taken aback for a moment, then switched hands to hold the dust whisk and bowed lightly, murmuring, “I will follow the master’s order.” 

Unable to resist, the old master asked, “Master, what about Uncle Jiang?” 

Once the master entered seclusion, no one could control that 'little Taoist boy' from the White Jade Capital. 

After all, this true monarch, in both seniority and cultivation, dared not intervene. The further apart the lineage, the harder it was to reason. 

The Great Heaven Monarch turned to glance at the old door, where a young Taoist boy sat on a mat, perusing a book while chatting with the sword immortal Zhang Lu, who was drinking nearby about trivial matters in the text. The Great Heaven Monarch hesitated a moment before saying, “Just let him be. Over the hundreds of years guarding the Inverted Mountain, Jiang Yunsheng has been quite honest. If he were back in his hometown, a few Inverted Mountains wouldn't suffice for his mischief. My little uncle dotes on him; every time he goes to the Grand Xuan Dao for trouble, he has to bring Jiang Yunsheng along. If it weren’t for Master Sun having murderous intent towards Jiang Yunsheng, my little uncle would’ve kept Jiang Yunsheng from having to seek refuge in this Haoran world.” 

The Grand Xuan Dao, the lineage of sword immortals, and one of the ten great sword immortals of the Qingming world, Sun Daoist. 

The old master sighed, “If Uncle Jiang survives this great calamity, he will surely have future blessings.” 

Fortune and misfortune are intertwined; with a different world, the fortunes might turn. Perhaps many years ago, when the ancestor brought Uncle Jiang to the Grand Xuan Dao to “make a scene,” it had provoked Sun Daoist's murderous intent, which was, in fact, deliberate. 

At Sun Daoist’s level, killing intent could be manifested as long as he was away from the White Jade Capital, especially close to his own Daoist temple, he could completely manifest the Dao and change his fortunes. 

The actions of the three-palm teacher ancestor might be called the brushstrokes of a deity. 

Of course, that presupposes they could safely escort Jiang Yunsheng out of the Qingming world. 

The Great Heaven Monarch had already entered seclusion, leaving the old master at the railing, gazing down at the entire Inverted Mountain. People only knew that the Inverted Mountain was the largest seal of a mountain character, but few realized that the catching-and-releasing pavilion and the elk cliff among the eight scenic spots, along with the solitary peak beneath him, formed an ancient formation inherited from the lineage of the Three Mountains and Nine Lords, ultimately crafting a presence akin to an ancient ascension platform. 

The old master, a disciple of the Great Heaven Monarch collected in the Haoran world, called this place home. However, he was quite similar to the old boatman who supported the three-palm teaching Lu Chen out to sea; for cultivators, where they were born was their first home, and where they practiced after ascending the mountain was their true home where their heart felt at peace. Thus, whether it was the old true monarch stationed at the Inverted Mountain or the old boatman wandering the seas year after year, both longed to go to the Qingming world to cultivate the Dao, but the Dao was high, and the journey was long; without someone to guide them, how could they ascend to another world? 

The old master watched as those sneaky cultivators infiltrated the Inverted Mountain, feeling it was rather pointless. Since the master had given the order to not interfere in anything, the old master operated his divine powers and directly manifested at the still of the night in the catching-and-releasing pavilion. In an instant, this true monarch, who had hunted countless dragons to refine his life dust whisk, appeared over the ocean. With nothing to do, he intended to take a distant look at the Dragon Valley. 

If it hadn’t been for Jiang Yunsheng saying something to this true monarch, all the true dragon descendants within the Dragon Valley should have perished long ago. The true monarch just needed to wait for the opportunity and intercept those rain-dispensing old dragons one by one; that dust whisk should have been an immortal-grade weapon. 

Little by little, he gathered equipment from the mountain, accumulating enough to successfully refine it into an immortal-grade weapon. This was the true monarch’s skill. 

Recalling that ancient secret, the old master stood atop the vast ocean, sighing deeply. 

Back then, the only one capable of persuading that sword immortal to sheath his sword was none other than Lu Chen. 

Beyond the Six Extremes, wandering in the land of No Where, amidst the vast wilderness. 

In communion with the spirits of heaven and earth, that three-palm teaching truly deserved to be called the “Ultimate Being.” 

It was no wonder that in this master ancestor’s eyes, all the immortal sects in the Haoran world were merely nests built by sparrows. 

The magical techniques of the immortal sect, capable of moving mountains and oceans, were nothing more than a mole drinking water. 

The more the old master reflected on the teachings of that three-palm teaching, the more he felt his insignificance; for a moment, he was somewhat dazed. 

The young Taoist boy exclaimed, turning to look at the high railing at the top of the solitary peak, calculating something with his fingers, utterly inexplicable. 

The sword immortal Zhang Lu curiously asked, “What’s wrong?” 

The young Taoist boy replied, “It’s somewhat like the gradual enlightenment and sudden realization of Buddhism; somewhat, but it still lacks a decisive wake-up call.” 

Zhang Lu laughed, “After accumulating hundreds of years of goodwill, can’t you lend a hand?” 

The young Taoist boy shook his head. “Not everyone can deliver a wake-up call. I certainly don’t have that skill. If I hit him slightly askew, the one who is only gradually realizing will end up with a head full of bumps.” 

Zhang Lu laughed, “Keep reading. Generally, whenever the little heavenly deity in the book stays by the lake or the deep pool, there’s bound to be a beauty bathing.” 

The young Taoist boy didn’t immediately turn the pages but suddenly said, “Take it easy. The other party has twice chosen not to go this way.” 

Zhang Lu grinned, “Still as sentimental as ever, huh? This kid probably won’t genuinely admire your Daoist teachings in his entire life.” 

The young Taoist boy shook his head, “It’s just about matters, not people. It’s not about that; pure feelings, pure nature, pure truth, and pure sincerity are all good seedlings for cultivating the Dao. In fact, our Daoist teachings are broader and deeper than you can imagine, higher and farther. You can’t dismiss our Dao just because my skills are lacking.” 

Zhang Lu yawned, “If you don’t turn the pages soon, I won’t last through the night.” 

The young Taoist boy began to flip through the book. 

Not long before this, a ferry boat from the Fuyou Continent had just sailed over a thousand miles from the Inverted Mountain when it suddenly received a flying sword message from one of the sect’s private residences. The old Nascent Soul cultivator pondered for a long time. Sure enough, the ferry’s sword room received many flying swords from fellow cultivators. In the end, after weighing the pros and cons, the old Nascent Soul cultivator chose to quietly leave the ferry and return to the Inverted Mountain. 

Not only the Water Cave but also several ferry talkers who had just left the Inverted Mountain had received messages from their respective channels, needing to return to the Inverted Mountain for an urgent matter. 

In fact, almost all the crossing ferries that had been near the Inverted Mountain or recently left were invited to Shao Yunyan’s Springfan Pavilion “as guests.” 

The invitee was neither Yan Ming nor Nalan Caihuan, but rather the “Sword Qi Great Wall.” 

This was an unprecedented oddity in the history of the Sword Qi Great Wall. 

This was no trivial matter that could be easily dismissed; many great merchants were curious about who would be the spokesperson for the Sword Qi Great Wall this time. Who had the qualification? Was it the old sword immortal Nalan Shaowei, who had once been schemed against by the then obscure ancestor of the Water Cave, only to end up in utter embarrassment? If it were this person, it would save them trouble. 

Thus, among all the cross-continental ferries that received the news, those from the Central Divine Continent and the Aiai Continent were the most numerous. Each sent someone to secretly return, mostly meeting halfway to speculate on the Sword Qi Great Wall’s intentions. There was certainly no danger to their lives; the Sword Qi Great Wall wouldn’t go insane. What they feared was if the Sword Qi Great Wall made a reckless move, causing complications and delaying everyone’s steady earnings. However, if they could decisively quell the Sword Qi Great Wall’s arrogance, it would be a great blessing for them all. 

Shao Yunyan, the owner of Springfan Pavilion, personally welcomed guests at the door, leading a stream of arriving guests to settle in various areas of the residence with a few remaining trusted elders. Shao Yunyan appeared amiable, and many ferry managers felt somewhat overwhelmed by the treatment. The sword immortal Shao Yunyan, owing to his treasured gourd vine, had many sects in the Haoran world and renowned sword immortals from across a continent owing him favors, thus making Springfan Pavilion incomparable to the Plum Blossom Garden or the Water Crystal Palace of the Rain Dragon Sect. Those who could stay at the Inverted Mountain were all undoubtedly wealthy, while those who could enter Springfan Pavilion often had achieved the Dao with bright prospects ahead. 

Springfan Pavilion had arranged over ten secluded courtyards, each gathering the talkers of the various ferries together. 

Before each person entered their courtyard, the sword immortal Shao Yunyan would smile and say, “Everyone, drink tea and wine for a moment, make yourselves at home. Just wait a bit, and we will go to the main hall of Springfan Pavilion to discuss matters together.” 

The old Nascent Soul cultivator Bai Xi from the Water Cave in the southwest of Fuyou Continent, unaware of what the sword immortal Shao planned, entered the courtyard and, upon stepping inside, saw someone sitting in the main room, looking up at him. 

Bai Xi's heart tightened, and he silently cursed. 

That person was none other than the sword immortal Xie Zhi from Fuyou Continent! 

He came from a genuine wild cultivator background; even after becoming a sword immortal, he still had no intention of establishing a sect and preferred to wander. Eventually, he ended up at the Sword Qi Great Wall, having had no interactions with any immortal sects in Fuyou Continent, particularly as Xie Zhi had never hidden his disdain for the Water Cave and had never even exchanged pleasantries with its ancestor. 

In the main room, several ferry managers, sharing Bai Xi’s feelings, sat stiffly, unable to relax. 

Xie Zhi’s first words made everyone uneasy. 

“Earning money through ability is good, but if you can’t spend it, that’s very bad.” 

Bai Xi suppressed his fear and displeasure, asking in a low voice, “Sword Immortal Xie, why do you say this?” 

Xie Zhi glanced at him sideways. “I’m a wild cultivator who eats from the mountains and fields; I can’t stand seeing those esteemed immortal teachers making big bucks. Is that reason enough?” 

Bai Xi was left utterly speechless. 

In another courtyard, a ferry manager from the Golden Armor Continent entered and also saw a woman with her eyes closed and a sword on her back sitting in the main room. 

Her looks were unremarkable, but what mattered was the long sword “Fuyou” behind her, renowned across the Golden Armor and Fuyou Continents, which involved an incredibly captivating backstory. To have a sword named after an entire continent, and for the sword’s owner not to be from that continent, how could there not be legendary tales? 

The woman sword immortal was Song Ping. 

Once, a great poet from Fuyou Continent saw Song Ping from afar and could not forget her for life. He longed for her for many years, passionately devoted, and never took a wife, writing poems in her praise that could fill a collection; among them, the line “I once saw you and dreamed of you again, your eyes like a bright light” was especially famous. Not only that, but he also wrote several poems in her tone, which were quite moving, bringing both laughter and pity. 

Inside, several old cultivators from the cross-continental ferries looked gloomy, and upon seeing the newly arrived kindred spirit, their expressions did not improve. 

They did not have the leisure and sentimentality of that poet, lost in longing. They felt that today’s reunion at the Inverted Mountain, this Springfan Pavilion, was easy to enter but difficult to leave. 

Song Ping opened her eyes, extended her two fingers, picked up a nearby wine cup, and drank it all in one go. “Have all arrived? Quite a few. Then let’s toast first; drink some wine before discussing matters.” 

When a sword immortal personally invites others to drink, they usually have to drink first. 

After the toasts, who knows if there will be any penalties for drinking? 

The sword immortal Pu He from the Northwest Liuxia Continent, a gaunt and tall old man, wasn’t seated inside but stood at the door, admiring the snow. A few old ferry cultivators could only stand in the corridor, watching the heavy snow fall. 

Pu He was once the most temperamental sword immortal of Liuxia Continent, killing based on whims. It was said he only stayed to hide and cultivate at the Sword Qi Great Wall after losing to another sword immortal in a duel. 

After waiting for everyone to arrive, he said, “You’re all businesspeople who like to trade, so since we’re all fellow countrymen, why not do me a favor? Will you sell or not?” 

The crowd exchanged glances. 

One person, gathering his courage, cupped his hands and asked softly, “May I ask if Sword Immortal Pu is speaking as a sword cultivator of the Sword Qi Great Wall or as a sword immortal of Liuxia Continent?” 

Pu He shot a sideways glance at this “uncooperative” Nascent Soul cultivator. “Get lost and send a message to your ancestor Li Xun that when I return to Liuxia Continent, I’ll bring a few friends and take my sword to visit your ancestral hall.” 

Before the Nascent Soul cultivator could salvage the situation, Pu He unsheathed his life sword, pointing the tip at the manager’s brow, as if to detain him on the spot, making him freeze in place. Then Pu He grabbed him by the neck and casually tossed him onto the street outside Springfan Pavilion, speaking with rippling intent, “Your ferry is called ‘Mizui,’ right? Looks rather flimsy; how about I help you replace it? Can a hiding, concealed Yu Pujing sword cultivator like Lingran protect you?” 

The ferry manager, who had been about to leave in resentment, stood frozen in place. 

This cross-continental ferry was vital to the sect, known for its size and strength, named Mizui because it had accumulated many magical treasures. Because of this, the sect had secretly hired a Yu Pujing sword immortal, Lingran, to be stationed there. However, aside from himself, no one else in the ferry knew about it, as that sword immortal rarely made his presence known. 

The Nascent Soul cultivator gritted his teeth and re-entered Springfan Pavilion, planning to apologize to Pu He. 

He wasn’t afraid of any actions from the Sword Qi Great Wall, as no one would die; it wouldn’t be specifically targeting him. However, he feared Pu He’s relentless approach would drag him and the whole sect into a fate worse than death. 

The four troublesome spirits on the mountain were the most difficult to deal with, especially the sword cultivators. 

Such a shameless sword immortal from his own continent, once they’d become entangled in a grudge, would undoubtedly be hard to shake off; it was quite evident. 

So, would such a favor be sold or not? 

Several managers from the Nansuo Continent were chatting merrily in a courtyard with their sociable sword immortal, Yuan Qingshu. 

Yuan Qingshu, unlike Pu He, Xie Zhi, and Song Ping, was very genial, not only bringing wine but also engaging in light-hearted conversation, saying that the Sword Qi Great Wall’s well-known bamboo sea cave wine was the best. He just mentioned one thing at the end: that his six direct disciples could visit the residences of the seated friends and serve as honored guests. As for today’s main business, there was no rush; they would go to the main hall to discuss after drinking. 

From the Aiai Continent, the number of ferry managers was quite large, second only to those from the Central Divine Continent. 

The female sword immortal Xie Songhua was rather peculiar. Growing up in Aiai Continent, she rose to prominence in the Central Divine Continent and never identified herself as an Aiai sword cultivator, claiming that a continent that couldn’t even hold on to the word “North” didn’t deserve her recognition as an Aiai person. 

Generally speaking, sword immortals with such a bad temper would struggle to thrive in the prosperous and renowned markets of Aiai Continent. After all, the immortal sects in Aiai Continent weren’t afraid of individual strong cultivators but could hardly resist the likes of Xie Songhua, who had several good sisters sharing her disdain for Aiai sword cultivators. One of them was a pure warrior fond of hunting demons in the frigid north, and she just happened to have a close relationship with the Liu family of Aiai Continent. 

Moreover, Xie Songhua had always looked down upon Aiai sword cultivators, but this time at the Sword Qi Great Wall, she surprisingly smiled at the younger generation, including Deng Liang. 

Once Xie Songhua saw seven or eight people take their seats, her opening statement was quite imposing. “I have drawn my sword twice at the Sword Qi Great Wall and have already achieved the merit of defeating a great demon at the Immortal Realm. Consider it a success and retreat.” 

This didn’t cause an uproar, but everyone’s heart sank. 

Currently, the Sword Qi Great Wall was on high alert, and information flowed very limitedly. Moreover, no one dared to investigate indiscriminately. However, one thing had already become common knowledge among travelers at the Inverted Mountain. 

It was indeed Xie Songhua’s sword that had destroyed a Yu Pujing sword cultivator’s foundation in the wild, and according to the rules of the Sword Qi Great Wall, such achievements equaled that of a half-immortal great demon. 

Moreover, this was the personal merit in the current offensive and defensive battle of the entire Sword Qi Great Wall. 

To be honest, the merchants from Aiai only felt a sense of pride in this connection, but what they truly sought was the business opportunities within it. 

Whoever could attract Xie Songhua to serve as a revered guest at the mountain gate would undoubtedly make a fortune! 

However, no one dared to speak up; everyone knew Xie Songhua’s temperament, and saying such a thing would just invite disaster. 

Why did everyone feel apprehensive? 

It was because this kind of indifferent sword immortal, who had no fixed residence, actively showing up to “talk business” could only mean trouble. 

Sure enough. 

“I owe someone a favor, so this time, returning to Aiai Continent, I’ll accompany you all.” 

What followed in Xie Songhua’s words sent chills down everyone’s spines. “He said, those who do business all want to earn as much as possible, and it’s reasonable; no faults can be found. He won’t hold it against you, and can even empathize with you. It’s impossible to have a deal where both parties can profit without any issues; if anything goes wrong, it’s not your fault, but his. So, you can not only relax, but you’ll also have unexpected rewards. After we finish discussing matters in the main hall, those of you who are short of money, those who are the most needy, I’ll personally escort this cross-continental ferry back to Aiai Continent, as it’s a favor I owe.” 

With a bamboo sword box slung over her shoulder, Xie Songhua looked at everyone, sneering, “If the escort doesn’t go well, it’ll be my fault for not being skilled enough.” 

The managers of the North Julu Continent gathered after everyone had arrived when they met Liu Caizhu, the master of the Floating Sword Lake. 

Everyone stood up respectfully, cupping their hands in greeting. 

It wasn’t because she was a Yu Pujing sword immortal or a sect master that warranted such heartfelt respect, but rather because Li Cai dared to come to the Sword Qi Great Wall, that was all. 

Li Cai did not take a seat; after returning the greetings, she picked up a prepared jug of wine and straightforwardly said, “Han Huaizi won’t be returning, and I should be leaving soon as well. That’s all said; let’s drink.” 

The sword immortal Wei Jin, seeing the two ferry managers from Longcheng, did not discuss business matters but asked about the recent situation in the Treasure Bottle Continent. He then said, “Once I ascend to the Immortal Realm, if I don’t die at the Sword Qi Great Wall, I will make a trip to the North Julu Continent to duel with Tian Jun Xie Shi once again.” 

The two old cultivators, already somewhat reserved, felt increasingly uneasy. 

The Eastern Treasure Bottle Continent was the smallest continent, while the sword immortal Wei Jin was regarded as an exceptionally rare talented sword immortal in the history of Treasure Bottle Continent. 

Who would dare to take it lightly? 

Once Wei Jin reached the Immortal Realm, the former leaders among the cultivators of the continent, such as the Shenzhao Sect’s Qi Zhen and the present one who had risen from a crossing dragon to a local snake, would have to reconsider their positions. 

In fact, the Longcheng ferry had recently received some credible news; the Yu Pujing sword immortal Wei Jin had already hit a bottleneck. 

Tonight, Wei Jin even confronted this barrier directly, making the two Longcheng ferry managers even more anxious. 

Wei Jin, with no ties or enmities, speaking to these two insignificant managers about breaking through was quite puzzling. 

Yet he certainly wished to inquire about the sword of Tian Jun Xie Shi. 

In the largest courtyard of Springfan Pavilion, all the ferry managers from the Central Divine Continent were present. 

Compared to the other courtyards’ tense and eerie atmosphere, the merchants and cultivators here appeared calm. Two older Yu Pujing cultivators, Wu Qiu and Tang Feiqian, were personally stationed there for their sect’s cross-continental ferry. However, they held no official capacity, as it would be too embarrassing. Among them, Wu Qiu was a sword cultivator accustomed to storms, and the two old immortals sat next to each other, chatting and laughing, their voices not low. 

Aside from their identities from the Central Divine Continent, the treatment by the Sword Qi Great Wall’s hosts simply could not suppress them. 

Just a Yu Pujing sword cultivator, Mi Yu, was two realms apart from the previously expected old sword immortal Nalan Shaowei. 

With the addition of Shao Yuan Dynasty’s sword immortal Ku Xia, who would help whom was still uncertain. Why did the Sword Qi Great Wall send such two people to host? This indicated that tonight in Springfan Pavilion, there would be no major upheaval. 

Wu Qiu and Tang Feiqian, both old cultivators of the fifth realm, felt a little more relaxed and began to scrutinize the young sword immortal Mi Yu and a female Nascent Soul cultivator beside him, who had excellent qualifications but insisted on becoming a ferry manager, which was a thankless task. Why was that? It was simply that she had fallen for someone. 

A lovesick person, unfortunate to fall for a romantic, was truly suffering. Why bother? There were countless talents in the Central Divine Continent; how could she be infatuated with a Mi Yu? 

If Mi Yu could leave the Sword Qi Great Wall and was willing to marry her, she would indeed be considered to have climbed high, but though Mi Yu was flirtatious, he was ultimately a sword immortal of the Sword Qi Great Wall; how could he possibly go to the Central Divine Continent? 

The sword immortal Ku Xia was not good with words. 

According to the prior instruction, he didn’t need to say much and just sat there as a mere companion. 

Wu Qiu turned to the nearby sword immortal Ku Xia and asked with a smile, “Where are Yan Ming and Nalan Caihuan? Are they waiting for us to finish our tea in the main hall?” 

Ku Xia shook his head, “Not sure.” 

Wu Qiu nodded, “No rush.” 

Although they were both Yu Pujing sword immortals, Ku Xia had an extra identity that made others not dare to belittle him. 

He was the nephew of Zhou Shenzhi, one of the ten of the Central Divine Continent. 

Regardless of how Zhou regarded this “foolish and incompetent” nephew, it wasn’t a reason for outsiders to look down on Ku Xia. 

The more the good-natured Ku Xia was, the less he should provoke enmity. 

Thus, it seemed that the Sword Qi Great Wall had wisely sent Ku Xia to host them; it was not an insignificant hand. 

However, once both sides began to negotiate finances, the face that Ku Xia would show might not hold much weight, after all, he wasn’t Zhou Shenzhi. 

Ku Xia sighed internally. 

In a while, when they saw that young man, it would be their turn to have headaches. 

With complicated feelings, the sword immortal Ku Xia even felt that if that day had come when the Sword Qi Great Wall faced off against that future ancestor of the Water Cave from Fuyou Continent, it shouldn’t have been the old sword immortal Nalan Shaowei but the young man who should be in the main hall of Springfan Pavilion now; it would be a good match. 

Because Ku Xia truly couldn’t imagine Lin Junbi would ever have a day of being subordinate to others. 

The female Nascent Soul cultivator spoke to Mi Yu through her heart, “Mi Yu, you will pay the price for this. I will risk the sect’s punishment afterward to make you lose face. Moreover, I may not even have to pay any price, but you certainly won’t be able to bear the consequences.” 

At this point, the girl’s tone had a touch of delight. “What a perfect example of ‘not getting revenge until the time is right’. Mi Yu, did you not expect that you would have this day?” 

Mi Yu looked at the girl, feeling regret, heartbroken, and spoke to her with heartfelt words in a quiet voice, “I never expected that the gentle girl back then would become so unlovable. I can only blame myself.” 

The girl was left speechless, her face growing even more resentful, her heart full of bitterness. Many words that nearly came to her lips seemed to shatter into pieces, and she could not utter a single word. 

To fall for someone and have deep feelings for a person, only to be unloved in return, felt as if one would never have a chance in this life. 

Mi Yu fell silent, his expression gloomy. He glanced at her, then turned his gaze away slightly, as if only daring to catch her out of the corner of his eye, able to see her but not daring to look directly. 

In the main hall of Springfan Pavilion. 

A young man leaned against the door, an ancient jade token hanging from his waist. 

Within, Yan Ming and Nalan Caihuan had already taken their seats, but both couldn’t sit in the master position at the four-sword table. Moreover, the positions of these two Nascent Soul sword cultivators were relatively far back. 

Nalan Caihuan felt somewhat awkward, while Yan Ming was indifferent. 

Earlier, she had been tricked by that babbling fellow once, and when Nalan Caihuan reported the details to Nalan Shaowei afterward, her ancestor had looked at her as if she were a fool for quite a while. Frustrated, Nalan Caihuan wanted to overturn all the agreements they had made, but unexpectedly, her ancestor instead told her to just let it be and proceed as discussed. 

Standing beside the young man was the owner of Springfan Pavilion, sword immortal Shao Yunyan. 

He didn’t mind whether he was being usurped. 

The two met for the first time and were chatting amiably about Liu Jinglong from the Northern Julu Continent and the Fairy of Watering River, Lu Sui, feeling quite compatible. 

Shao Yunyan said that Liu Jinglong had a promising Dao ahead of him and was likely to become the first ascended sword immortal of the Northern Julu Continent. 

The young man remarked that the Fairy Lu was gentle and understanding, a perfect match for Liu Jinglong, and casually praised Lu Sui’s master. 

Shao Yunyan was indifferent to whether the words were sincere; after several hundred years, even if it was just polite conversation, it was still nice to hear. 

The heavy snow of the Inverted Mountain continued to fall without pause. 

Beauties and heavy snow have always made a perfect pair throughout history. 

After chatting about the gourd vine and the fine wines of the Yellow Liang blessed land, Shao Yunyan asked, “Should we call them over now?” 

The young man smiled, “Not in a rush; we can’t let the sword immortals make a wasted trip to the Inverted Mountain. Let those who are used to dealing with immortal money feel more of the sword immortal’s grace.” 

Shao Yunyan nodded, “It’s about time.” 

The previously chatty young man fell silent on this matter, merely placing his hands within his sleeves, lightly tapping his fingers together, gazing up at the heavy snow. 

If only each snowflake were a piece of money. 

Shao Yunyan also looked up, enjoying this rare moment of tranquility. 

Last year’s old dream, I dreamt of being by my side, feeling suddenly in a foreign land. 

This year’s new dream, I suddenly arrived at the old mountain head of Watering River, seeing her still smile like a flower. 

The young man suddenly said, “Sword Immortal Shao, after tonight’s matter, regarding the issue you promised the Sword Qi Great Wall in the past, we can negotiate to change it. The matter remains the same, but the outcome can be different. No party will be put in a difficult position.” 

Shao Yunyan frowned and asked, “You have the final say?” 

The young man smiled, “I don’t have the final say; who does?” 

Shao Yunyan felt a sense of relief. 

Originally, the sword immortal, who had already decided to die at the Inverted Mountain, took a few steps back and cupped his hands in gratitude to the young man. 

The young man accepted it calmly, extending his hand from his sleeve to return the salute. 

As long as it didn’t involve life and death, Shao Yunyan felt unburdened. He then offered, “As for business matters, let’s count it as a share of Springfan Pavilion.” 

The young man immediately placed his hand on Shao Yunyan’s arm, saying, “How righteous! Truly sword immortal grace. This snow wasn’t a waste, I’ve been waiting for your words for a long time.” 

Shao Yunyan was caught off guard. 

He sensed that the group of merchants would face a terrible disaster tonight. 

For aside from the hosts, there were now two additional sword immortals returning from viewing the scenery, Sun Juyuan and Gao Kui. 

In addition, there was sword immortal Mi Yu from the Sword Qi Great Wall. 

From the Central Divine Continent, Shao Yuan Dynasty’s Ku Xia. 

From the Nansuo Continent, Yuan Qingshu; from the Northwest Liuxia Continent, Pu He; from the Golden Armor Continent, Song Ping; from the Southwest Fuyou Continent, Xie Zhi; from the Aiai Continent, female sword immortal Xie Songhua; and from the North Julu Continent, the master of Floating Sword Lake, Li Cai. 

And the great sword immortal Wei Jin from the Treasure Bottle Continent. 

A large group of sword immortals from the Sword Qi Great Wall and foreign sword immortals suddenly left the Sword Qi Great Wall and gathered at the Inverted Mountain. 

This was an unprecedented event in the history of the Sword Qi Great Wall. 

Shao Yunyan bid farewell and entered the room first, taking a seat in his chair, which was quite near the main door. 

Tonight, none of the sword immortals visiting the Inverted Mountain were from the Tongye Continent. 

Because Tongye Continent was the only continent without cross-continental ferries, nor did it have sword immortals practicing at the Sword Qi Great Wall. 

It was quite a coincidence. 

However, the man who had nodded at the Great Heaven Monarch now had his sword Qi reined in, quietly leaving the Inverted Mountain with a mid-fifth realm sword cultivator from Tongye Continent. They were headed for the now most destitute Tongye Sect of Tongye Continent, not to ask about swords this time, but to help draw swords. This would aid not only Tongye Continent but also the Haoran world. If not for this, would he ever wish to leave the Sword Qi Great Wall, letting his junior brother remain behind alone? 

Scholars fear righteousness the most. 

Zuo, who had always considered himself a scholar from the mountains, was not some sword immortal from the mountain. 

More importantly, once he arrived at Tongye Continent, he could draw his sword more freely and perhaps even fight alone, without any sword immortals beside him. 

His junior brother had schemed, wanting him to go to Nansuo Continent, claiming that the situation there would be the most perilous. However, after hearing a certain little brat’s words, he decided to go to Tongye Continent instead. 

His junior brother must be regretting it immensely. 

Chen Qingdu had been in high spirits at the time. 

This journey would be long. 

They would not make any stops along the way through Dragon Valley or the Rain Dragon Sect. 

Only pausing slightly at Lu Hua Island to confirm whether it was truly the legendary high being of the Daoist sect or the so-called hidden great demon of Cui Dongshan. 

If it were a high being, they could sit and discuss the Dao; if it were a great demon, they could cut it down with a sword. 

Zuo rarely faced any difficulties. 

This time, accompanying Zuo was a young Golden Core sword cultivator from Tongye Continent, named Wang Shizi. Though young, he was of similar age to Zuo and not particularly old. 

This young Golden Core cultivator, Wang Shizi, was a wild cultivator; at this age, becoming a Golden Core sword cultivator could be considered a genius. 

Unfortunately, upon arriving at the Sword Qi Great Wall, he found no fellow countrymen and felt quite awkward in a place full of sword immortals. With a low realm, he felt out of place, and aside from Wei Jin from Treasure Bottle Continent, he had no other sword cultivators to interact with, so he naturally didn’t dare to approach Wei Jin for casual conversation. 

In his ten-plus years at the Sword Qi Great Wall, he had truly spent most of his time in solitary cultivation, with minimal returns from hunting demons on the city walls, just enough to support his stay. 

However, things had improved slightly in the past two years, as he had often gone to a small tavern to buy wine. Without friends or companions, unless there were few customers, it was hard to get a seat to drink; he could only squat by the roadside, sipping wine and eating plain noodles. Compared to his past loneliness, this was truly a better experience. 

To return to his hometown this time was a tremendous surprise; he never expected to travel with the great sword immortal Zuo. 

Nonetheless, Wang Shizi understood the stakes and remained silent throughout the journey. 

As they approached Dragon Valley, Zuo said, “There’s no need to be overly cautious; if you have any doubts about your cultivation, just ask.” 

Wang Shizi replied softly, “I’m still at a low realm; it’s not a big deal. I can wait until we reach Tongye Continent to ask.” 

Zuo did not press this peer sword cultivator further. 

Zuo turned back to glance at the direction of the Inverted Mountain. 

The night was thick, and between heaven and earth, the snowflakes fell like jade, shimmering brighter than silver mercury. 

Wang Shizi curiously asked, “Why would you, a senior, choose to leave the Sword Qi Great Wall at this time but still be willing to actively teach me sword techniques?” 

Zuo withdrew his gaze and laughed, “A wild cultivator of Tongye, Golden Core guest Wang Shizi, alone for fourteen years, has climbed the city walls thrice and been forced to retreat thrice. I, Zuo, consider you a fellow cultivator, so when I speak of sword techniques with you, it’s not just guidance; it’s sparring.” 

Wang Shizi was left speechless, several times wanting to speak but hesitating. 

Zuo said, “Speak freely.” 

Wang Shizi smiled, “I thought it was the second shopkeeper speaking with me.” 

Zuo laughed heartily, “I’m a senior brother of Chen Qingdu; if you think our words and actions are similar, it’s not strange.” 

Wang Shizi said, “Senior, I believe the second shopkeeper will definitely make a name for himself in the Haoran world!” 

Zuo shook his head, “Just wait; the Haoran world will only blame him for not doing enough. All those past grievances will become reasons for criticism. The door-closed disciple of the Wensheng lineage, the younger brother of Zuo, Chen Qingdu, will also be a person worth taking note of. What a new hidden official who has distanced himself from the battlefield—this will all serve as excellent excuses to deny my younger brother. If he dies, it should be expected, so it won't be mentioned. But as long as he doesn’t die at the Sword Qi Great Wall, it will always be a thousand mistakes.” 

Wang Shizi felt heavy-hearted. 

Zuo said, “It’s not surprising; you’ll get used to it.” 

Zuo and Wang Shizi continued to ride their swords eastward, leaving no further words. 

Before leaving the Sword Qi Great Wall, Zuo had shared heartfelt words with Chen Qingdu. 

“Chen Qingdu, are you truly not the least bit disappointed?” 

“Merely comforting a young man who hasn’t completely lost hope. Disappointed? Not disappointed? To say I’m not disappointed would be true; there’s no hope left to lose.” 

At the Inverted Mountain, in the Springfan Pavilion. 

The layout of the main hall at Springfan Pavilion still followed the etiquette of the scholarly families of the Haoran world. 

A large painting of an immortal landscape hung in the main hall, depicting an unknown mountain peak from the Northern Julu Continent, with couplets on either side containing Confucian teachings on self-cultivation and family governance. Above it hung the plaque “Liubei Hall.” 

In front of the wooden wall was a long table, with a four-sword table in front of it and two rows of chairs on either side. 

Between the entrance and the wooden wall, facing each other, were arranged several chairs in orderly fashion. 

When the guests entered, they would find a small world within this space upon sitting down. 

The managers and talkers from the various ferry routes arrived one after another in this hall. 

After Bai Xi from the Water Cave sat down, he exchanged glances with a few old friends, not daring to communicate through heart voice, but a hint of worry was evident in their eyes. 

The arrangement of the chairs in the hall was quite significant. 

The sect’s foundation, the size of the ferry and trade, and the personal reputation of the ferry talkers seemed to have been calculated thoroughly. 

For instance, Bai Xi noticed that the manager of the “Nanjizi” ferry from the Aiai Continent was an inconspicuous Golden Core cultivator who had always traded in medium-sized businesses. During social interactions, he was someone who wouldn’t say much even at the drinking table. Yet, today, his seating arrangement was notably high. Bai Xi, having learned from the ancestor of the Water Cave, knew this person was actually a concealed Yu Pujing talisman cultivator, whose dealings in the cross-continental ferries were simply a facade; instead, he would sneak off to Dragon Valley to conduct transactions using immortal money, exchanging it for opportunities to extract dragon essence with his unique secret techniques, which he would then resell at high prices to the Liu family of Aiai Continent. 

The ancestor told Bai Xi to pay attention to this character; there was no need to make a deliberate connection, just to be mindful of his gaze and words upon meeting. 

Bai Xi could assert that this “Golden Core old cultivator” appeared calm on the surface but was certainly feeling quite uncomfortable underneath. 

Eventually, everyone took their seats. 

Over ten sword immortals who had left the Sword Qi Great Wall sat on the right side, while the seats directly opposite were even more sparse, with each continent’s sword immortal facing a ferry manager. 

Thus, until this moment, the dozens of ferry managers began to reexamine the young man. 

Every guest present had their own business acumen, being old foxes who had long since honed their trading skills. They had all noticed this somewhat out-of-place young man, who had been gazing up at the hanging couplets in the spacious Springfan Pavilion. 

Wu Qiu and Tang Feiqian, two old gods of the fifth realm from the Central Divine Continent, had keenly observed this young man, and after gauging him, they couldn’t help but feel perplexed. They wouldn’t genuinely believe he was merely a lower fifth realm cultivator, calculating in their hearts, unconsciously treating him as a young, well-concealed sword immortal. 

The four-sword table beneath the plaque remained unoccupied, except for a jade token placed on it, positioned closer to the ferry manager from the Haoran world. 

Not only Wu Qiu, but nearly everyone began to speculate that one of the two seats might be occupied by the sword immortal Han Huaizi of the Taihui Sword Sect, followed by a big sword immortal as the finale, perhaps Nalan Shaowei or one of the heads from the Dong, Chen, or Qi families? Otherwise, why would so many sword immortals gather here? 

Unfortunately, it was now exceedingly difficult to obtain information from the Sword Qi Great Wall. 

Moreover, no one dared to act rashly or independently. 

Even a friendly sword immortal like Sun Juyuan had long since started to refuse guests and later made his way to the city walls, with all the servants in his residence either following the sword immortal to the city walls or being confined indoors. Once, someone thought this wasn’t necessary; soon after sneaking out, they died. 

Thus, the information circulating about the Inverted Mountain was merely that which the Sword Qi Great Wall felt was unnecessary to conceal. 

Once everyone settled, the opposite sword immortals had already taken their seats. 

Different sword immortals exhibited different temperaments, seating postures, and auras. 

Even Wu Qiu felt a suffocating sensation. 

Unbeknownst to them, they were all facing the array of over ten sword immortals! 

The critical point was that those who were clearly from the Haoran world were now all presenting themselves as sword cultivators of the Sword Qi Great Wall. 

Except for the Central Divine Continent and Northern Julu Continent, the ferry managers of the other six continents, who had previously been hosted by their own sword immortals, were already feeling quite tense. They never expected that it would be even more excruciating here. 

After all, the dozens of ferry managers from all the continents had seen many storms, but who could personally experience such a situation? 

All the sword immortals had gone mute. 

This kind of atmosphere usually only existed before a sword immortal decided whether to take a life or not. 

There was no need for words when a flying sword could take a head. 

In the hall. 

The owner of Springfan Pavilion, sword immortal Shao Yunyan, sat near the entrance, not speaking. His position ensured he would definitely not be the first to speak tonight. 

Yan Ming and Nalan Caihuan showed no signs of speaking either. 

All the sword immortals remained silent. 

Mi Yu, Wei Jin, Sun Juyuan, Gao Kui, Yuan Qingshu, Xie Songhua, Pu He, Song Ping, Xie Zhi, Li Cai, and Shao Yunyan. 

Along with two Nascent Soul sword cultivators, Yan Ming and Nalan Caihuan. 

Some older managers, growing more cautious with age, began to perspire. 

Were they perhaps to be wiped out entirely? 

One cautious manager stole a glance at the two empty master positions. 

Another manager surveyed the young man standing by the towering column. 

The young man coincidentally made eye contact with him and smiled slightly. 

The old manager’s smile was forced, his face stiff. 

The young man remained silent until he spoke, his words crashing like a mountain into a lake, creating waves of shock. 

He walked at a measured pace toward the master position, cheerfully saying, “Since everyone is here, let’s start discussing matters.” 

Upon hearing these words, even some of the previously languorous sword immortals began to sit up straight. 

As he reached the master seat on the right side of the four-sword table, Mi Yu was the first to stand. 

Eleven sword immortals, two Nascent Soul sword cultivators, nearly all stood. 

The dozens of managers hurriedly rose in a panic, with some who stood up a moment too late wishing they could slap themselves twice. 

One by one, they were still in a state of confusion, yet they couldn’t ignore the intimidating stance of the sword immortals. 

Once the young man took his seat, all the sword immortals finally settled down. 

The young man extended a finger and lightly tapped the table, causing the jade token to flip over and reveal the ancient seal characters for “Hidden Official.” 

In the hall, one could hear a pin drop. 

All the businesspeople seeking wealth at the Inverted Mountain quickly shifted their gazes from the jade token, holding their breath, focusing their minds, as if facing an enemy. 

The young man, whose identity had finally become clear, smiled and introduced, “Allow me to introduce myself. My name is Chen Ping’an, the newly appointed Hidden Official of the Sword Qi Great Wall.” 

(End of Chapter)

 ### Chapter 747: Moving Mountains and Draining Seas

The Hidden Official of the Sword Qi Great Wall? Isn’t that the legendary girl with the sheep horn braids? It is said that she could shatter the true forms of great monsters across the wilderness with just her bare fists, making her the most combative of all.

How did she become this unfamiliar young man standing before them?

Even if they didn’t want to believe it, they had to now. With so many sword immortals present, there was no way this young man could simply spout nonsense. 

Or rather, even if they refused to believe, they had to pretend to. Otherwise, if they were to lose their heads to the flying swords of the sword immortals from this continent and have their corpses tossed into the Upside-down Mountain, who would bear the grudge? Could they band together in outrage and seek vengeance from the Sword Qi Great Wall? They should remember that those in the same trade are often rivals. Many ferry businesses actually conflicted with one another.

An old steward from the Aiai Continent weighed the situation before standing up, bowing slightly, and saying slowly, “Congratulations to Sword Immortal Chen on your promotion to Hidden Official. I am Dai Minghao, the steward of the ‘Tai Gang’ ferry on Aiai Continent. My cultivation level is hardly worth mentioning; I fear it would dirty the ears of the Hidden Official. I dare to say, tonight's meeting is a great honor for us, as it is a privilege to have the Hidden Official in attendance. When the Hidden Official speaks, how could we dare disobey? There is really no need to trouble so many senior sword immortals to attend. I am dull and blind, and currently unclear about the developments of the war at the Sword Qi Great Wall. I only know that any sword immortal here is a peak powerhouse with immense killing power. If they stay at the Upside-down Mountain for even a moment, they will have to spend much less time drawing their swords—what a pity!”

Wu Qiao raised the corner of his mouth, then let it drop again. 

Dai Hao’s words had both soft and firm tones, setting a good precedent. He was indeed a Golden Core guest on the path of cultivation and a shrewd businessman.

With so many renowned sword immortals present, instead of discussing business with us minor merchants, it would be more fitting for them to head to the Sword Qi Great Wall to slay monsters.

That suited the demeanor and style of the sword immortals better.

Wu Qiao felt he ought to show some gratitude towards the ‘Tai Gang’ ferry, after all, Dai Hao was taking a considerable risk to speak up on behalf of all the ferries across the eight continents. 

If a sword immortal were to suddenly go on a rampage and kill, Wu Qiao would certainly step in to stop it.

Sitting across from the steward of the Aiai ferry was the female sword immortal Xie Songhua, who raised an eyebrow. 

What a surprise! The Aiai Continent she was responsible for had become the first to jump out and disrupt the proceedings as a “seeker of swords”? 

Chen Ping’an had been patiently listening to the old Golden Core’s speech, his gaze fixed on the words hidden within Dai Hao’s speech. He then gestured to Xie Songhua, indicating that it was not a big deal, just a minor matter.

Chen Ping’an nodded to the old Golden Core steward, smiling as he said, “First of all, I am not a sword immortal. Whether I am a sword cultivator is open to interpretation. If you are interested, you can take a guess. I have taken many cross-continent ferries, and I know that for long journeys, if there isn’t something to alleviate the tedium, it can be quite unbearable. Secondly, among those truly qualified sword immortals present, like the sword immortal Xie sitting opposite you, when to draw their swords and when to retract them is not something outsiders can advise on. It is a good thing that good-hearted people are willing to speak sincerely. Dai Hao, you have set a good example. Moving forward, as we discuss matters, we should be candid and straightforward.”

This made many ferry stewards, who initially thought the young man would be humiliated and lose his temper, feel somewhat disappointed.

Chen Ping’an paused lightly, tapping the table gently, his smile unwavering. “But ultimately, it’s about being able to manage what cannot be managed. Don’t say it’s me; even our senior sword immortal doesn’t constrain himself. Why? It’s simple: sword immortals are ultimately sword immortals; both body and mind are free to draw their swords. Otherwise, how could one be the leader of the four difficult spirits of the mountains, if not for never caring much about matters of divine money, sage principles, or sect rules?”

The steward of the “Wapan” ferry from the Fuyang Continent, Bai Xi, sat opposite the sword immortal Xie Zhi, who had a wild cultivation background.

The steward of the Jin Jia Continent’s ferry was opposite the woman sword immortal Song Ping, who had earlier poured a drink before serving punishment alcohol.

Across from them on the Liuxia Continent was the sword immortal Pu He, who had once tossed a Yuan Ying ferry steward out of the Spring Banner Pavilion like a chick and had said he wanted to gather a few friends and reminisce with Li Xun at the Ancestor Hall.

The ferry stewards of these three continents were particularly moved by the new Hidden Official’s words.

Chen Ping’an maintained a friendly demeanor, as if he were chatting with acquaintances. “Dai Hao, I appreciate your good intentions, but if someone from another continent were to say these words, it would be more appropriate. Coming from you, it feels a bit out of place. The sword immortal Xie has drawn her sword twice: once obliterating the foundation of a Jade Purity realm monster sword cultivator, and another time completely destroying an ordinary Jade Purity realm monster, leaving nothing behind. As for the Yuan Ying and Golden Core monsters, naturally, they would have been eliminated as well. Therefore, the sword immortal Xie has achieved a complete merit and will not return to the Sword Qi Great Wall; instead, she will leave the Upside-down Mountain with you to return home to Aiai Continent. Regarding this matter, did the sword immortal Xie not mention it earlier while busy reminiscing with her fellow townsfolk?”

Chen Ping’an turned to look at Xie Songhua.

Xie Songhua stared at Dai Hao intently and said, “I’ve mentioned it. I reckon that Old Daoist Dai has forgotten.”

Chen Ping’an waved his hand, casting a glance at the heavy snow falling outside the Spring Banner Pavilion, and said, “No worries, let’s just consider it as mentioning it again. It’s a rare thing to encounter fellow townsfolk in a strange land, so it’s worth reminding once more.”

Dai Hao stood up, clearly not daring to sit back down, as he likely would feel like he was sitting on needles if he did. 

“Why are you standing? Everyone is seated, and standing alone might seem as if you are looking down on the sword immortals,” Chen Ping’an said, his smile fading as he addressed the old Golden Core. “Sit.”

Dai Hao immediately sat back down. 

Wu Qiao and the neighboring Tang Feiqian, both from the Middle Earth’s Jade Purity realm, exchanged quick glances. 

It seemed this new Hidden Official was not very sword immortal-like.

The concealed Jade Purity cultivator from Aiai Continent’s “Nanji” ferry, Jiang Gaotai, was quite elderly yet maintained a youthful appearance. His seat was very close to the front, adjacent to Tang Feiqian. He had some connections with Dai Hao from the “Tai Gang” ferry, and since he’d been directly exposed by the Sword Qi Great Wall, he was worried that the business of the Jiao Long Ditch would be disrupted in the future.

This prompted Jiang Gaotai to speak up, both for public and private reasons, as it was only natural to say a few words. Otherwise, would a whole continent like Aiai truly allow Xie Songhua, a woman, to grip their throats?

Without even standing, Jiang Gaotai directly spoke, “Hidden Official, we are of no worth in terms of cultivation level. If it comes to the skills of killing, perhaps all of us added together, with a couple of sword immortals joining forces, would wipe out all the guests in this Spring Banner Pavilion.”

Xie Songhua narrowed her eyes, raising one palm and lightly stroking the armrest of her chair.

Jiang Gaotai ignored this and continued, “We, who are full of copper smell, are good only at engaging in minor businesses to earn a meager living. If the Hidden Official thinks it’s worth discussing, then let’s talk properly. If not, we will endure any unsuitable business to survive. I can’t concern myself with how others from different continents think. I, Jiang Gaotai, have a tattered ‘Nanji’ ferry and will take the lead. Hidden Official, just set the price. Even if it’s a loss-making business, I will still engage, celebrating the fact that Sword Immortal Chen has been promoted to Hidden Official of the Sword Qi Great Wall.”

Wu Qiao, Bai Xi, and others all looked at Jiang Gaotai with newfound respect. 

He was clear and decisive. 

Wu Qiao’s only worry, for now, was not the young Hidden Official with a smile masked by a blade, but rather the internal conflicts among “their own,” such as the longstanding grudges with Beiju Lu Continent and Aiai Continent. 

Earlier, Shao Yunyan of the Spring Banner Pavilion personally arranged for the ferry stewards of one continent to gather in a courtyard and host guests with the sword immortals from their own continent, which could be said to be quite scheming. 

The animosity between Beiju Lu Continent and Aiai Continent was well-known. 

Thus, an old Yuan Ying sword cultivator steward from Beiju Lu Continent wanted to immediately tear down Jiang Gaotai’s “high ground.” Even if he hadn’t shared a drink with the leader of the Floating Weeds Sword Lake, just because a little brat from Aiai Continent was showing off, Beiju Lu Continent would be inclined to retaliate. The order of speaking from the two ferry stewards of Aiai Continent had made them think that Beiju Lu Continent was dead?! 

In the world of Haoran, Beiju Lu Continent was the only one with cross-continent ferries heading to the Upside-down Mountain, and they made the least profit!

However, all ferry stewards, including the old sword cultivator within, had received the message from Li Cai, “Don’t pay attention to this guy; tonight’s meeting is just for show.”

Chen Ping’an smiled and said, “It’s proper etiquette to stand and speak in Haoran.”

Upon hearing this, most of the ferry stewards opposite the sword immortals changed their expressions. 

Let Dai Hao sit down and then let Jiang Gaotai stand up? 

Didn’t the logic already belong to Chen Ping’an alone? 

Jiang Gaotai’s expression darkened. He had generally had a smooth life, with continuous opportunities. Even when dealing with bigshots from the Liu family of Aiai Continent, he had never faced such an insult, only receiving respect.

Chen Ping’an clasped his hands into his sleeves and watched Jiang Gaotai with a smile.

Dai Hao had stated that he did not wish to waste the sword immortals’ time slaying monsters, and the young Hidden Official had said quite a bit of unrelated things. The truly weighty words were that Xie Sword Immortal had shattered the Yuan Ying Golden Core of a Jade Purity realm monster. The Golden Core in question was Dai Hao’s old Golden Core? 

Jiang Gaotai’s retreat was a forward move, clearly denying the sword immortals the chance to take action while also testing the bottom line of the Sword Qi Great Wall. In the end, the young Hidden Official spoke about the proper etiquette of Haoran? 

Many old stewards felt extremely uncomfortable, as these matters were not the way they were best at discussing.

Jiang Gaotai smiled and stood up, cupping his fists. “It was my lack of etiquette, and I apologize to the Hidden Official.”

Wu Qiao, Tang Feiqian, Bai Xi, and others secretly breathed a sigh of relief. 

They truly feared Jiang Gaotai might give that young man the chance to demonstrate his authority. 

Unexpectedly, that young man smiled again, “Accepting the apology means you can sit down and talk.”

The dignified Jade Purity realm cultivator, Jiang Gaotai, stood there with a dark expression. 

If he were to engage in a business duel with the young Hidden Official, no matter how difficult it would be to endure privately, Jiang Gaotai was a businessman and wouldn’t be so embarrassed. What really worried Jiang Gaotai was losing face tonight at the Spring Banner Pavilion, only to be flayed and trampled afterward, which would affect many of his private trades with the Liu family of Aiai Continent.

Jiang Gaotai pretended to be unwilling to be used as a pawn and was about to leave in a huff.

Xie Songhua said, “Hidden Official, I will take the ‘Nanji’ ferry back home now, no need to see me off.”

Unexpectedly, Shao Yunyan was even more resolute. He stood by the door and said, “The Sword Qi Great Wall and the Nanji ferry, even if the business doesn’t work out, we still have our righteousness. I believe the Hidden Official won’t obstruct it. As an outsider, I shouldn’t concern myself with these matters. It just so happens that I, Shao Yunyan, am the owner of the Spring Banner Pavilion, so before Sword Immortal Xie leaves, allow me to accompany Jiang shipmaster for a stroll through the Spring Banner Pavilion.”

Shao Yunyan didn’t want Xie Songhua to act too extreme, fearing it would affect her future path to greatness. He was alone, so he didn’t care.

Jiang Gaotai stopped in his tracks, laughing heartily, and turned to look at the young man with a smile. “Hidden Official, do you think we are fools? Does the Sword Qi Great Wall really welcome customers and do business like this? I want to see after half a year of this coercive buying and selling, how many ferries will still be docked at the Upside-down Mountain?!”

Chen Ping’an smiled and said, “Shipmaster Jiang is a very clever person; otherwise, how could you have reached the Jade Purity realm? You must know proper etiquette. You probably never wanted to do business with us from the start. No matter, I’ll let Jiang shipmaster leave, and let Master Shao accompany you to enjoy the scenery. So as to avoid any misunderstandings, I want to mention something here: Sword Immortal Shao has no relations with us, and tonight’s meeting is held at the Spring Banner Pavilion, which I paid for on behalf of the Sword Qi Great Wall.”

Shao Yunyan smiled and said, “With the arrival of sword immortals, such a small place as the Spring Banner Pavilion is honored, so there is still a discount.”

Chen Ping’an sighed, displaying a somewhat mournful expression as he spoke to Jiang Gaotai, “That big hat of coercive buying and selling, I can’t bear it. If the Sword Qi Great Wall cannot do business with the Nanji ferry, even if it pains me to death, I can only blame my own lack of ability. It’s just a pity I didn’t even get the chance to make an offer. Shipmaster Jiang didn’t even want to hear my price. It really goes to show the old saying—when one is insignificant, their words hold little weight. I would rather be tactful. Let everyone enjoy a good laugh.”

Chen Ping’an stood up, looking at Jiang Gaotai, who still hadn’t moved. “I won’t hold it against you for being impatient, and you shouldn’t misunderstand my sincerity. Instead, don’t throw mud at me; gentlemen end their friendships without harsh words. In the end, let’s settle for a courteous parting.”

Then Chen Ping’an no longer looked at Jiang Gaotai and shifted his gaze to Wu Qiao, Tang Feiqian, and Bai Xi, saying, “The Sword Qi Great Wall treats guests with great sincerity. Dai Hao has spoken, and Jiang shipmaster has also spoken. Next, there’s one more person who can say something before the Sword Qi Great Wall. After that, I’ll come back to discuss business. The principle is always the same: from today onward, if I allow you ferry operators to earn less than before, this kind of business—let’s not talk about doing it, even if I wanted to, I wouldn’t.”

At this point, Chen Ping’an turned his attention to the sword immortals, “Sword Immortal Xie, wouldn’t you accompany Jiang shipmaster to send him off?”

Xie Songhua stood up and looked at the young Hidden Official who had personally helped her accumulate two feats. This woman, who was most reluctant to owe favors, surprisingly showed a hint of guilt.

Chen Ping’an gently shook his head.

Xie Songhua broke into a smile, no longer wanting to be coy, and turned to Jiang Gaotai, saying, “Once I step outside this door, I’ll just be Aiai Continent sword cultivator Xie Songhua. Shipmaster Jiang, let me and Master Shao, two sword cultivators of your level, accompany you to stroll through the Spring Banner Pavilion?”

Jiang Gaotai’s mind raced as he asked, “Hidden Official, are you truly not going to let us lose money? Is that real?”

Chen Ping’an walked around the four-sword table, pressed his hand against the jade plaque with the ancient inscription “Hidden Official,” and faced both sides, smiling without saying a word.

Shao Yunyan had already walked towards the door.

Xie Songhua had already exuded a hint of sword intent, and the bamboo sword box behind her trembled.

Tang Feiqian stood up, slightly turning to the young man, cupping his fists and saying, “I sincerely request Hidden Official to keep Jiang shipmaster; parting unhappily is ultimately not pleasant. If Hidden Official is willing to allow the Nanji ferry to exert a small effort, wouldn’t that be even better?”

Tang Feiqian was not helping Jiang Gaotai to save his life; he was, in fact, helping himself and everyone present who was nervously doing business with the Sword Qi Great Wall tonight. 

All the resentment had to be hidden for now. 

Once they left the Spring Banner Pavilion, far from the Upside-down Mountain, everything would be negotiable.

Chen Ping’an asked, “The scenery on the mountains of Haoran is winding and familiar to you, and I am no stranger. Not discussing business, but Shipmaster Jiang, what do you think will happen when you step out the door? Do you think you, Jiang shipmaster, know what’s at stake? Why should you stay? As the third person to speak with me, please express your thoughts well; I will endure for a moment and listen.”

Chen Ping’an lightly tapped the jade plaque with his fingers, smiling as he said, “In this hall, discussing business has its own rules, and those rules will always outweigh my status as Hidden Official. In the end, it’s all business dealings, and grievances can be resolved over divine money. Once you spend some time with me, you will naturally understand that I am one of the fairest businessmen of the Sword Qi Great Wall.”

Sword Immortal Xie Zhi smiled and said, “That’s true.”

Chen Ping’an immediately added, “Helping one’s own people speak will only hinder them.”

Xie Zhi glanced at the ferry stewards from Fuyang Continent. “Hidden Official, you are right, but I, Xie Zhi, am from Fuyang Continent, and the people here are my wealthy relatives.”

Wei Jin from the Wind and Snow Temple, sitting with a blank expression, closed his eyes to meditate, feeling somewhat helpless at this point. 

The words from the wild cultivator sword immortal Xie Zhi didn’t seem like something Chen Ping’an had taught him beforehand. It seemed like genuine words spoken in the heat of the moment.

Tang Feiqian pondered a moment before cautiously saying, “As long as the Hidden Official is willing to keep Jiang shipmaster for discussions, I am willing to make an exception to take action and offer a 10% discount on the next ferry docking at the Upside-down Mountain.”

Chen Ping’an took the jade plaque and hung it at his waist before returning to his seat, saying, “Why should I allow a foolish Jade Purity realm person with money to continue sitting here and make things difficult for themselves? Do you think my title of Hidden Official is worth less than a ‘Nanji’ ferry that only steals a bit of dragon energy in the Jiao Long Ditch? Ten percent? The Liu family of Aiai Continent sells the dragon energy to your Tang Feiqian’s backers, which is only worth a ten percent profit? You already look down on me; do you also look down on Jiang Gaotai’s fundamental survival?!”

Tang Feiqian frowned. 

How did the Sword Qi Great Wall know about such private matters? 

Chen Ping’an said solemnly, “The Sword Immortal of Ku Xia.”

“Here,” the Ku Xia sword immortal prepared to stand.

If Xie Songhua owed Chen Ping’an a big favor, then the Ku Xia sword immortal’s association with the Shao Yuan Dynasty was a debt greater than a huge favor. 

As the future pillar of the Shao Yuan Dynasty, Lin Junbi had a bright path ahead!

The Ku Xia sword immortal was straightforward—repay one favor for another, simple as that. 

If he couldn’t return it, since he was the disciple of Zhou Shen Zhi, he could always let Lin Junbi take a few messages back to the Central Earth Divine Continent after returning.

As for whether his master, Zhou Shen Zhi, would listen to his nephew’s final words, whether to take action or not, the Ku Xia sword immortal didn’t want to think too much about it.

Bai Xi knew that as long as the sword immortals present were the most agreeable, if this person began to threaten, it would be severe trouble for their side.

Thus, even if Bai Xi had to steel himself, he needed to stop the Ku Xia sword immortal as the steward of the Wapan ferry from the Mountain and Water Cave, and he would speak first! 

Bai Xi had seen through the situation; dealing with this young Hidden Official, who was more righteous than Haoran, couldn’t involve any tricks.

Bai Xi stood up with a calm expression and said, “If Hidden Official insists Jiang shipmaster leaves, then let it be one for me, Bai Xi of the Mountain and Water Cave.”

Bai Xi even smiled, not hiding his sarcastic intent. “I only hope that Sword Immortal Xie and Sword Immortal Shao wouldn’t think that my cultivation is too lowly and thus unworthy to accompany you.”

Xie Songhua simply responded with an “oh,” and casually said, “Not worthy is not worthy, but that’s fine. I have plenty of sword intent in my bamboo sword box.”

Shao Yunyan stood by the door.

The wild cultivator sword immortal Xie Zhi turned to look at the young Hidden Official. 

Chen Ping’an smiled and gestured for him to remain seated, indicating that there was no need to get up and speak.

With Bai Xi unexpectedly willing to break the deadlock with his own life, they wouldn’t be led around by the nose by the Sword Qi Great Wall any longer. Soon, there were other cultivators from the same continent familiar with Bai Xi who also stood up, “Count me in.”

Even the Yuan Ying ferry steward who had been tossed out of the Spring Banner Pavilion by Pu He earlier, despite having earlier been treated like a dog by the sword immortals, resolutely stood up and said, “I, Liu Yu, shipmaster of the ‘Fuzhong’ ferry, would also like to enjoy the sights of the Spring Banner Pavilion, along with experiencing the sword intent of Sword Immortal Xie.”

Not only that, but there was also an unnamed young Golden Core female ferry steward, who had a special identity as a fairy from the Southwest Sea of Haoran. Her seat was quite far back, yet she stood up and said, “I, Liu Shen, shipmaster of the ‘Ni Chang’ ferry, wonder if there is a chance to join Sword Immortal Xie and Sword Immortal Shao on a tour of the Spring Banner Pavilion.”

The lowest cultivation level was still that of a female cultivator.

This method of death had its significance.

The last to stand was the Yuan Ying female cultivator who had earlier conversed with Mi Yu. She slowly rose, smiling at Mi Yu, “Sword Immortal Mi, it’s an honor to meet you again. I wonder if your sword technique has improved after many years.”

Mi Yu smiled and said, “I can’t bear to.” 

The Yuan Ying female cultivator sneered.

Wu Qiao, who had been motionless, felt immensely satisfied. 

This is how the ferry operators from various continents should conduct business with the Sword Qi Great Wall, showcasing their “small world.” 

Aren’t sword immortals most fond of and skilled at killing? 

Now there were people, and not just one, stretching their necks to see if they would truly be killed. 

Would they draw their swords or not? 

Jiang Gaotai cupped his fists and said, “Thank you, everyone!”

Tang Feiqian, who had stood up and hadn’t sat down, shared a similar feeling as his friend Wu Qiao. 

Did this young Hidden Official really think that calling a large group of sword immortals to pressure them, relying solely on a piece of jade plaque, meant everything was under his control? 

What an ignorant brat! 

At such a young age, what was he even worth! 

Li Cai extended a finger, rubbing her mouth corner, wanting to slay one with a sword to put an end to the matter. 

However, the voice of the young Hidden Official echoed in her heart, urging her to remain calm. 

Only then did she manage to refrain from drawing her sword. 

Wei Jin had opened his eyes. 

The two old Dragon City ferry stewards who had been about to take action immediately became obedient. 

The ferry masters from the Southern Powsa Continent remained relatively quiet. 

As for those from Beiju Lu Continent, they had no intention of getting involved at all. 

At this moment, after the fervor of sentiments had passed, everyone gradually noticed that the young man, who should have been in a precarious situation, had actually propped his head on one hand, leaning back against the four-sword table, smiling as he watched everyone. 

Beiju Lu Continent, Baoping Continent, Southern Powsa Continent—all negotiable. 

One was due to ancient customs, one was too difficult to communicate with, and one was too close to the Upside-down Mountain, especially with that erudite Chen clan, and Chen Chun'an had only just left the Sword Qi Great Wall not long ago. 

The Central Earth Divine Continent, Aiai Continent, and Fuyang Continent were the hardest to negotiate with. 

One was used to pointing fingers and looking down on the heroes of the eight continents. One believed that divine money was more important than anything. One was the one most experienced in the business of the Upside-down Mountain and also the most capable of making money. 

Whether Jin Jia Continent and Liuxia Continent were negotiable or not depended on the situation. 

Currently, it had become a situation that was not very negotiable. 

Chen Ping’an’s gaze finally lingered on the two old Dragon City ferry stewards for a while longer. 

The cross-continent ferries from Baoping Continent were essentially just the six ferries from Dragon City, the Fu family’s Treasure Swallowing Whale, and that floating island known as the “Little Upside-down.” The Sun family had a mountain sea turtle that had been captured and tamed by their ancestors, and the Fan family also had that Osmanthus Island. 

The two stewards visiting the Spring Banner Pavilion tonight were one from the Fu family’s Treasure Swallowing Whale and one from Ding family’s cross-continent ferry. 

Having been to Dragon City several times, he had never met either of them, and it was likely that even if these two big shots from Dragon City had heard of “Chen Ping’an,” they would just think it was a common name. 

The young Hidden Official lazily smiled and said, “What’s the deal? A good mutually beneficial business transaction has to be placed on the table like this, weighing it by the pound? I don’t think it’s necessary.”

Tang Feiqian coldly laughed, “Just now, you were shouting for blood, trying to use the sword immortals’ might to dictate life and death, as if we were the ones doing it.”

Chen Ping’an maintained his posture, smiling as he said, “Am I not young and brash, with a little power going to my head, getting a bit carried away?” 

Wu Qiao took a sip of tea from the Spring Banner Pavilion and gently set the cup down, smiling, “We people have not achieved much in our lives, and we are worlds apart from the Hidden Official. We are not from the same path, so we are unable to converse on the same wavelength. It is indeed difficult to make a living, and each of us puts our lives on the line. Why don’t we change the location and time to talk again? Still, that saying holds true: a Hidden Official’s words carry weight. There’s no need to trouble the sword immortals; perhaps it would suffice to have the head of the Yan family or Sword Immortal Nalan deal with us little people.”

Chen Ping’an smiled and said, “I mentioned before, there are rules for stepping out, and there are rules for sitting here. For example, everything can be resolved over divine money. Earlier, there was quite a commotion, and you didn’t think it through. So I want to clarify: I came to the Upside-down Mountain to change a large number of ferry masters, for example…”

Chen Ping’an looked at the young Golden Core female cultivator sitting at the back, “‘Ni Chang’ shipmaster Liu Shen, I am willing to offer two hundred Gu Yu coins or equivalent goods from the pill workshop to have your junior sister take over ‘Ni Chang.’ The price may not be fair, but if a person is dead, what can be done? After all, the ferry can still earn two hundred Gu Yu coins. Why did I pick you first? It’s simple: you’re a soft persimmon, and when it comes to killing, your mountain peak and master won’t even dare to let out a whimper.”

The Golden Core female cultivator’s face instantly turned pale. 

Jiang Gaotai immediately asked with a smile, “I wonder how much my head is worth in the eyes of the Hidden Official?”

Chen Ping’an shook his head and said, “You are a sure death, no need to pay me a single divine coin. The Liu family from Aiai Continent will handle the mess. As for the Central Earth Divine Continent, the Ku Xia sword immortal will also speak to his master Zhou Shen Zhi to settle things with Tang Feiqian and his backing. Everyone is in business, and it should be clear that levels of cultivation aren’t that important.”

Chen Ping’an said, “Sword Immortal Xie, don’t go out just yet. If Jiang shipmaster says another word, just kill him. This way, they won’t think I, the Hidden Official, wouldn’t dare to use a heavy hand.”

Xie Songhua exhaled heavily. 

Finally, she could draw her sword and kill someone. 

Chen Ping’an turned to Bai Xi, the Yuan Ying from the Mountain and Water Cave, and said, “Your ancestor has old grudges with our Sword Qi Great Wall, and the hatreds run deep. The previous Hidden Officials ignored you, but I’m here now. Tonight, don’t leave. I’ll have Sword Immortal Xie make an extra trip to protect your Wapan ferry, ensuring a smooth return to the Fuyang Continent’s Mountain and Water Cave, and clarify with your ancestor that all grievances will be settled. After that, business will continue as usual; whether you come or not will be up to you, and the consequences will be yours to bear.”

This time, it was the sword immortals who began to stand up. 

The wild cultivator sword immortal Xie Zhi stood up, smiling and reminiscing, “It has been many years since I’ve killed a bureaucratic immortal; how nostalgic.”

Chen Ping’an continued, “As long as you haven’t stood up to leave, everyone here is a distinguished guest of the Sword Qi Great Wall.” 

Chen Ping’an smiled and said, “Without bringing all the details and some of the petty grievances to the surface, letting the ferry owners and the Sword Qi Great Wall see each other clearly, how can we build long-term trust for business?”

Chen Ping’an said, “Mi Yu.”

Mi Yu stood up, his expression cold, looking at the female Yuan Ying cultivator, “I’m sorry; this last time was my final deception. I can actually afford it.” 

The Yuan Ying female cultivator’s heart felt like it was being sliced apart. 

Then Mi Yu pulled out a booklet from his sleeve, glancing around, casually picking a steward who hadn’t yet stood up but had almost done so earlier, revealing the family lineage of that person. 

Not just their origins and which disciple of theirs was favored, but also how their descendants branched out at the foot of the mountain and where their various private residences were located—not only their private properties at the Upside-down Mountain but also their residences across the continent, even noting those like Wu Qiao and Tang Feiqian who had foundations in other continents, all meticulously recorded. 

Mi Yu spoke freely about the details of those relationships and connections, including with which fairies they were not spiritual partners yet had connections that were even closer than that. 

After mentioning two ferry stewards’ backgrounds as if he were counting his treasures, Chen Ping’an said, “That’s enough; no need to go on.” 

Mi Yu nodded. 

Now that he had been appointed by the Hidden Official as the leader of the Hidden Officials, it wasn’t for nothing, was it? 

Chen Ping’an called out another name, “Pu He.” 

Pu He stood up, staring at the Yuan Ying cultivator who had previously apologized to him, his eyes dark. “I just can’t understand. How can there be such a trader in the world who almost died and wants to die again? I want to see if that Jade Purity realm Ling Ran will kneel on the ground and beg me for a favor once I board the ship.” 

Chen Ping’an looked at the key figures from the two ferry stewards from the eight continents, “Wu Qiao, Tang Feiqian. You two old immortals have even purchased houses at the Beiju Lu Continent’s Dili Mountain, yet you still call yourselves small fries in front of me.”
