Earlier, on the way Mi Yu came, he felt a bit out of place, asking a question, “If I feel out of place, don’t those sword immortals feel out of place? Do they know these jade tokens are being given to these bastards?”

“They know; I’ve made it clear to each sword immortal,” Chen Pingan’s response was simple, “What’s there to feel out of place about? In the future, every time someone sees a jade token, they’ll mention the names and deeds of the sword immortals, their surnames, names, realms, and the great feats they accomplished, slaying which major demons. Perhaps even better than you, Mi Yu, could recite them by heart.”

Mi Yu immediately chuckled bitterly, “Hidden Official, I’m also a sword immortal! Why didn’t you mention it to me beforehand?”

Chen Pingan laughed, “Many sword immortals who agreed without a second thought have asked me in person whether there is any of Mi sword immortal’s sword energy among these jade tokens. I said no, and they were relieved. What do you want me to do? You think you should be treated differently just because you’re a prominent figure in the Hidden Official lineage? If I tear out the page for you in the ledger and place it at the front, would it make a difference? If you feel it would help and make you feel better, you can tear it out yourself and place it near Yue Qing or your brother Mi Hu’s pages. I could pretend I didn’t see it.”

Mi Yu felt a heart-wrenching pain as he felt his sincere feelings being crushed. 

At this moment, he felt no sense of awkwardness whatsoever. 

He only regretted that he couldn’t participate in this.

At that moment, everyone in the great hall had carefully tucked away their jade tokens.

This caution was not only due to the rare treasure they were being treated to, but also worry about inadvertently triggering the jade tokens to explode alongside the sword energy, or fearing that their actions would reveal their movements, or that all their words and deeds were being observed by the young Hidden Official. After all, every gentleman in the Confucian Academy bore such a jade token for this purpose.

Mi Yu felt a surge of emotions, recalling some of the guidance that the young Hidden Official had given him on the way here.

“With these merchants, no matter how much you sweet-talk them, bringing up old friendships, or promising benefits for the future, it’s all empty words.”

“Need to see the big picture through small examples.”

“We don’t need to explicitly state that they can obtain something from the Sword Qi Great Wall through this jade token. Let them guess for themselves. The answer that clever people come up with will be reliable enough, regardless of whether it’s right or wrong.”

The discussions in the great hall became smoother, with more disputes laid on the table, which didn’t necessarily mean it was a bad thing.

Until dusk, the meeting came to a temporary pause.

During this time, the various plots, the eight continents’ ferry boats jointly plotting against the Sword Qi Great Wall, one continent’s ferry boats banding together to plot against neighboring continents, and the various ferry boats within a continent plotting against one another. Mi Yu was truly not interested, but due to his responsibilities, he couldn’t avoid getting involved, making him realize for the first time that focusing on sword training wasn’t such a苦差事.

Everyone dispersed again, returning to their courtyards for secret discussions. In truth, after most of the sword immortals had left, the communication through words and thoughts in the great hall was already stable enough. However, having such a process still eased the hearts of the ferry boat managers crossing continents, at least making them feel more at ease. Otherwise, frequently glancing at the empty seats where the sword immortals had sat would create an invisible pressure that made it uncomfortable.

Chen Pingan continued to wander alone around Chun Fan Zhai, agreeing to reconvene for discussions in two hours.

However, Mi Yu, the sword immortal, had matters to attend to.

Because the young Hidden Official had instructed Mi Yu to carry out two tasks.

Facing those young sword cultivators in the summer palace, Mi Yu still felt somewhat superfluous. He hadn’t anticipated that upon arriving at the Hanging Mountain, the burdens on his shoulders would be quite heavy.

One task was to privately visit the boat owners and mention the words “gifts should be reciprocated.”

He had to subtly hint that this was a personal favor from the Hidden Official, not part of the large-scale dealings between the ferry boats and the Sword Qi Great Wall.

You, Mi Yu, would be responsible for receiving the gifts. Yan Ming and Nalan Caihuan would not be suitable for this task.

Mi Yu then inquired about the final destination of these benefits.

Chen Pingan stated frankly that all would have to be handed over to Yan Ming and Nalan Caihuan. However, before that, all the sword cultivators from the Hidden Official lineage would have the opportunity to pick one cherished item.

Mi Yu curiously asked if he would also get a share.

Chen Pingan laughed, “Of course, if you really can’t help but pity the beautiful, you can return two personal items from that Nascent Soul female boat owner back to her; consider it as you, Mi Yu, prepaying your reward.”

Mi Yu was greatly impressed; in this world, the one who understood him best was the Hidden Official.

The other task was to find Yan Ming and Nalan Caihuan, so the three of them could come up with a catchy name for this Chun Fan Zhai meeting that would make all the ferry boat owners feel proud, making it seem like a grand event rather than one of coercion. At the very least, it shouldn’t let others think so.

They needed to ensure that everyone felt that discussing matters at Chun Fan Zhai was an excellent topic worth bragging about. As long as they got off to a good start, even if these merchants left the Hanging Mountain, all the ferry boat managers would naturally help promote and build momentum behind the scenes. Some of the small boat owners who originally had to hand over the jade tokens to their sects could conveniently keep them as private treasures.

The Qi practitioners of the Haoran world all care about face, so they would give them that; after all, the Sword Qi Great Wall and the Hidden Official lineage wouldn’t have to spend a single coin.

A total of eleven sword immortals personally came to host the guests. 

The boat owners had previously endured great hardships at Chun Fan Zhai, and after they left, as long as both sides had an unspoken understanding and a tacit agreement, once it was handled properly, these boat owners would have the chance to earn immense prestige, becoming a part of this grand tale.

Chen Pingan was truly just wandering around, casually crafting a large snowball hidden among nearby items, intending to give it to Guo Zhujiu, as the current Sword Qi Great Wall was sweltering in the heat.

Lingzhi Zhai would probably see booming business over the next few days.

This was a matter for the sects and schools, which could be noted down in accounts, but it was expected that everyone would still need to dig into their pockets to offer a decent piece of magical treasure, as gifts should come in pairs for good fortune.

An hour and a half later, Mi Yu returned to see the young Hidden Official.

Chen Pingan smiled and joked, “If the other party didn’t agree, it’s better than agreeing, granting you a free friendship? In the end, did she have autumn water-like eyes and scold you, telling you to roll out? But with your level of cultivation, you should have successfully kept that treasure.”

Mi Yu helplessly said, “Hidden Official, if you spent a little more effort on women, it would be incredible. I ended up leaving that treasure at the door.”

Chen Pingan hesitated for a moment, “Since I had you do two tasks, I’ll still give you another treasure. Once you return to the Sword Qi Great Wall, you can choose one to give to your brother.”

Mi Yu felt awkward once more.

He knew this was the good intentions of the Hidden Official and understood that his brother Mi Hu would feel pleased seeing him achieve a little something within the Hidden Official lineage, at least not just surviving.

However, Mi Yu ultimately found it difficult to do such things.

There are too many such small matters in life—saying thank you to someone, or apologizing to someone, is just something he can’t do.

The two walked side by side, and Chen Pingan slowly said, “I’m not asking you to deliberately play tricks to please your brother. If that were the case, I’d be squandering the efforts of you two and myself. A person calculates many things ultimately for the sake of not calculating too many matters. Your awkwardness stems from whether your thoughts or your brother Mi Hu’s thoughts are more important. You still haven’t figured it out. If we’re talking about giving and receiving, can you afford to owe Mi Hu? If Mi Hu weren’t burdened by you, he would have already been a great sword immortal alongside Yue Qing. Yet now he’s just breaking through to become an immortal, why is that? The entire Sword Qi Great Wall knows the answer. I suggest you see Mi Hu, not for anything else, but to let your brother know that all your efforts and sacrifices, Mi Yu, are acknowledged and you won’t play dumb.”

At this point, Chen Pingan didn’t want to sound too serious, so he joked, “Just be a bit more shameless; when you see Mi Hu, just say, ‘Brother, I don’t expect to reach the immortal realm in this lifetime, but for the sake of the old Mi family’s lineage and blossoming, I will definitely be significant within the Sword Qi Great Wall. In the future, those little fellows who call you uncle will definitely not be just one or two.’”

Chen Pingan concluded, “This is just my outsider’s perspective; how you actually feel is still very important.”

Mi Yu chuckled, “I also think… it seems pretty good. I’ll give it a try later.”

After Mi Yu left, Chen Pingan walked along a stone path where mountains and waters met, separating the artificial hill from the spring, the path covered with colorful pebbles that must have come from immortal mountains. Chun Fan Zhai didn’t often have many guests, so the pebbles were barely worn, reminding Chen Pingan of the Jade Crystal Cliff in the Chun Lu Garden of the North Ju Lu continent.

Coincidentally, Shao Yunyan was not far away, holding a delicate porcelain basin and tossing fish bait into the water.

Chen Pingan walked over, leaning against the railing as he watched the fish compete for food, saying, “How many little fish are in the blue waters.”

Shao Yunyan smiled, “Elegant and to the point.”

After a moment, Shao Yunyan asked, “Are there still worries at present?”

Chen Pingan nodded, “I’m worried that among the ferry boat managers, the sects have long conspired with the savage world, and I fear the conspiracy is deep enough that they would risk their lives to destroy the Chun Fan Zhai alliance. I’m also worried that some unexpected individuals from the Hanging Mountain might resort to brute force. Regardless of which concern arises, once it happens, no matter what the truth is, the result presented to the world will be that people have died under the swords of immortals from the Sword Qi Great Wall. The ferry boat owners from the Fuyao and Aiai continents, especially Bai Xi from the Mountain Water Cave, have a higher likelihood of dying, and afterward, there will be plenty of nasty excuses that can be made, leading to chaos among the people, rendering all previously agreed matters null and void.”

Shao Yunyan questioned, “After doing so much, even if people die, there are loopholes everywhere that can’t withstand scrutiny. Can it really reverse the situation?”

Chen Pingan reached out to wipe away the snow on the railing, “People’s hearts don’t operate on so many rationales. Building a table and bench takes painstaking effort, but to smash it, isn’t it just a few hits?”

“To scheme against others, one must be prepared to be schemed against.”

Then Chen Pingan smiled and countered, “What if I hypothesized further: someone indiscriminately leaves the Hanging Mountain and starts a massacre against those ferry boat owners? Would they dare dock at the Hanging Mountain again in the future?”

Shao Yunyan’s expression grew solemn, “Regarding this matter, it seems it’s not right to speak to the ferry boat owners, but not speaking is also not right. If we say it, everyone will be inclined to profit and avoid harm; if we don’t say it, once something happens, they will never return.”

Chen Pingan leaned against the railing, “So, it’s not about fearing the unexpected, but about fearing an unexpected event that is clearly lurking in the shadows. As long as the other party is patient and doesn’t act, I can only accompany them until they tire.”

Shao Yunyan asked, “How to respond?”

Chen Pingan sighed, “Then I need to meet that great Tian Jun; hopefully, I won’t be turned away at the door.”

Shao Yunyan’s face took on a strange expression, “I just received news that he has already gone into seclusion.”

Chen Pingan rubbed his forehead, feeling a headache coming on, contemplating for a moment, “That’s fine; it’s almost like he’s helping me make a decision. I’ll accompany Sword Immortal Shao to the third candidate for the South Posa continent.”

It would be the female sword immortal, Lu Zhi.

In fact, the merits she had accumulated were already enough for her to leave the Sword Qi Great Wall.

It seemed she was more interested in traveling and training her sword in the savage world rather than in the Haoran world.

The premise was that she was willing to leave the Sword Qi Great Wall and take a position at the Hanging Mountain.

Otherwise, it wouldn’t matter if the title of Hidden Official was useless; it would be equally meaningless to bring out the great sword immortal.

However, even if Lu Zhi agreed to this matter, her early departure from the Sword Qi Great Wall would actually have considerable impact.

In reality, it was a matter of weighing the lesser of two evils.

Chen Pingan gently tapped the railing, discussing countermeasures with Shao Yunyan.

Should they leak some details about the Chun Fan Zhai meeting, to create an early impression and intentionally leave only Mi Yu, to entice the other party to weigh their options and act immediately?

Should they notify Xie Songhua, who had already gone to the Jiaolong Gully and Yulong Sect? With Lu Zhi, Mi Yu, and Xie Songhua, plus Shao Yunyan, the higher the opponent's realm, the better. Even a ferocious Ascended Realm demon would not escape calamity.

Two days later, the young Hidden Official returned laden with gifts and received quite a bit.

Sword Immortal Mi Yu remained at Chun Fan Zhai.

There’s no wall that doesn’t leak wind in this world.

The discussions at Chun Fan Zhai, within a single night, set the entire Hanging Mountain abuzz.

The general content revolved around the Sword Qi Great Wall negotiating the larger situation with the ferry boat managers; one side would provide swords, and the other side would provide money to jointly respond to the current sieging war from the savage world.

Mi Yu, Shao Yunyan, and Xie Songhua were hidden within three directions of the ferry boats. Even those three ferry boats had no idea about this, managing to allow a sword immortal to “escort” them.

The Southwest Fuyao continent, South Posa continent, and Eastern Baoping continent.

Quietly arriving at the Hanging Mountain, Lu Zhi would take charge there, ready to assist any sword immortal who might wander far.

On the “Wapan” ferry boat of the Fuyao continent, Bai Xi sat in the cabin, frowning slightly when a knock was heard at the door.

Before this Nascent Soul cultivator could open the door, an old man appeared within, removing the illusion to reveal a young man looking languid.

Bai Xi stood up and solemnly asked, “I didn’t know a senior was visiting. What business do you seek?”

The young man smiled, “Not quite a senior. I’m Bianjing, a small sword cultivator from the Central Land, here to ask about the details of the Chun Fan Zhai meeting, and to decide whether to start a massacre.”

Bai Xi fell silent.

The young man’s eyes turned pitch black as he wrote a line on the table, then said hoarsely, “Your ancestor from the Mountain Water Cave is an old friend of mine. That fate-defining magical treasure was once an opportunity I gave him. The words on this table should be told to every ferry boat manager before they die; don’t you find it strange why every ferry boat manager dies shortly after leaving their post? It’s all to hide this strange little secret. You, kid, have the best luck; born late, you have the chance to meet me and gain a massive fortune for free. This unbreakable Nascent Soul bottleneck of yours will naturally be broken with ease upon meeting me.”

Bai Xi immediately cupped his fists and bowed, “Welcome, senior!”

“Bianjing” took a seat and smiled as he asked, “You and the ferry boats, wouldn’t you be unaware if someone had acted against you?”

Bai Xi did not sit down and remained standing, saying, “The ferry boats have already been thoroughly searched, especially my residence. There’s absolutely no possibility of tampering, and as for that jade token, I left it in the private residence at the Hanging Mountain. Additionally, all my actions and words are reasonable; I even purposefully complained a bit afterward, merely for show for Chun Fan Zhai’s watching. That crafty young Hidden Official wouldn’t find any trace, and instead would dismiss any doubts.”

Bianjing smiled, “What jade token? Young Hidden Official? Tell me more.”

Bai Xi recounted the general idea of the jade token, receiving a great compliment from the young man in front of him for the thoughtful arrangement, although it was a pity it wasn’t meant for their world, and then proceeded to carefully describe the process of the Chun Fan Zhai discussions.

Bianjing nodded, “If this succeeds, it’ll be a huge problem; it was worth the risk of me coming here.”

After saying this, Bianjing burst into laughter, “You thought I was at the Immortal Realm, but you’re mistaken.”

Bai Xi once more cupped his fists in salute.

An Ascended Realm great demon!

Bai Xi cautiously asked, “Senior, when do you plan to strike?”

Bianjing glanced at this little ant, Bai Xi, who had the guts to speak, and slowly began lifting him off the ground, “You should ask for the ferry boat to be sunk after you strike, letting more die is no issue. Otherwise, our Mountain Water Cave would be highly suspected; it would only delay your future actions and greatly affect the situation.”

Bianjing nodded with a smile, “That’s a good point. Since you’re so clever, you’ve truly gained a great fortune.”

The Southeast Tongye continent had plans laid, but unfortunately, it was exposed early, only leaving the Fuji Sect and Taiping Mountain injured. One of the plans from the Southwest Fuyao continent was this Bianjing, who was born from Fuyao continent yet traveled to the Central Land, risking much to deceive that national teacher of the Shao Yuan dynasty. Fortunately, this young sword cultivator “Bianjing” chosen by himself was quite capable.

As for the South Posa continent, with Chen Chun’an present, it wouldn’t be worth the risk of death; there were no plans there.

Bianjing said, “I won’t rush to act; the risks are too great. The ferry boats scattered back to their homes, I won’t act against them for now. I’ll wait until the next time they earn more money and happily walk to their deaths.”

Bai Xi breathed a sigh of relief; this indeed was a safe course of action.

Otherwise, he would truly fear this senior would act recklessly relying on his Ascended Realm cultivation.

Bianjing chuckled, “That young man named Chen Pingan is smarter than you can imagine. There’s a jade purity sword cultivator hidden on the ‘Nishang’ ferry boat, should be the little lackey sword immortal Mi Yu you mentioned. I’m just here for a leisurely trip, no rush at all; I’ll accompany them for a bit longer. I want to see how patient these prideful sword immortals can be. If their patience is indeed good, I’ll just wait longer to strike.”

Bianjing’s smile faded as he stood up, Bai Xi feeling as if he were being choked, slowly being lifted off the ground, “You are just an ant; don’t blame others.”

Bianjing sneered, “Chen Pingan, you’re willing to exchange your life for mine? What are you thinking?!”

Outside the door, a familiar voice Bai Xi knew well seemed to be speaking on his behalf.

“Don’t blame others for being foolish.” 

Bianjing laughed, “Chen Pingan, you’re actually willing to risk your life to change mine? What are you thinking?!”

Outside, a young man, cursing and swearing, tore off the mask of a woman’s face.

Next to him stood Lu Zhi, who hadn’t removed her male disguise.

In addition, both of them bore the illusion cast by the great sword immortal Chen Qingdu.

Bianjing inquired, “How did you follow me?”

The young Hidden Official smiled, “Just like the Mountain Water Cave, gamble big to win big.” 

Just as Bianjing was about to make a move, he suddenly froze.

Because an elder in a Confucian robe, who should not have appeared here, showed up.

Bianjing laughed heartily, “Good good good! Not only have several sword immortals come, but you even invited Chen Chun’an!”

The old Confucian scholar replied indifferently, “My name is not one that you can call.” 

*(End of Chapter)*

 ### Chapter 750: Wandering Souls, All Like Dandelions

The reason Chen Pingan dared to show himself wasn't just because he stood beside Lu Zhi, one of the top ten sword immortals of the Sword Qi Great Wall; more importantly, it was because Chen Chunan would be present.

In a battle of similar realms, while a great sword immortal excels at killing, they may not be as adept at saving lives.

Earlier, on the city wall, during that ambush, Mi Yu had exerted every effort to stop his fellow sword immortal who had an equal cultivation level, yet he was still a moment too late.

As long as Chen Chunan was there, however, there was no cause for concern.

After Chen Chunan spoke, he didn’t give the ascendant demon any chance to waste words. The world itself seemed to shift.

In an instant, Chen Pingan felt his spirit tremble, as if he had manifested an immense dharma form. Suddenly, he "ascended" to the highest point of the sky, able to overlook the entire expanse of the majestic realm. However, before he could take in the view, his vast dharma form was forced back into a speck smaller than dust, returning to the earth as if it had vanished into the intricate patterns of a palm.

When Chen Pingan finally regained his bearings and turned to look back, a phrase from a Daoist scripture naturally surfaced in his mind: "The Dao is elusive, hazy and indistinct, merging into the true void; the great emptiness is it."

Behind Chen Pingan hovered a massive orb, pure white and radiant, with faint outlines of pavilions and a large osmanthus tree, as if it were the moon itself adorned with fragrant flowers.

In comparison, Chen Pingan appeared as small as a grain of rice next to this celestial being.

He withdrew his gaze and looked up, where a colossal sun hung in the sky, even larger and wholly golden, with nothing else in sight.

This great sun continuously emanated strands of golden light, fluctuating and shifting rapidly.

There was also a small black dot, flitting erratically like an ink blot.

Countless thin white rays of light flashed through the air, capable of severing those golden threads in an instant.

It was likely that this was Lu Zhi confronting the ascendant demon known as "Border."

Chen Pingan hesitated for a moment, planning to sit cross-legged and immerse himself in this small realm, summoning his yet-to-be-named personal flying sword to engage with the grand flow of this microcosm’s Dao.

Unexpectedly, someone placed a hand on his shoulder and said with a laugh, "Some knowledge, if accessed too early, can be quite detrimental. It’s not that I fear you might steal it; it’s that the powers of your personal sword and my arts are not aligned within the same Dao."

Chen Pingan dismissed the thought and turned to respectfully bow to the elderly scholar in the Confucian robe.

Chen Chunan nodded and smiled, "I’ll just consider this a junior scholar paying respects to an elder. It’s not as if I’m a disciple from the lineage of the Sage of Literature, nor will I exchange formalities with you over our respective teachings."

After Chen Pingan stood up, he felt a flush of embarrassment. "I dare only to seek guidance, not to ask for the Dao."

Chen Chunan waved his hand dismissively, "Since we both share the surname Chen, we are of the same origin but different branches. Our surname is but a reflection of this, and the same goes for our scholarly pursuits. Furthermore, regarding the osmanthus tree in the Li Pearl Cave, the Chen family of the Yingyin region owes you a favor. That’s why I brought you in to observe the battle from a distance. To appreciate the prowess of a sword immortal is no small skill of yours. While I don’t worry about Chen Pingan of the Longquan County, I do keep an eye out for that old scholar and his proud disciple. Isn’t that 'just as expected'?"

Chen Pingan felt increasingly ashamed.

Chen Chunan reached out and pulled the sword immortal Mi Yu, who was outside the realm, into their midst.

Chen Chunan then reminded him, "Can’t see clearly? You might as well quietly contemplate your teacher's scholarly principles; perhaps your vision will clear up a bit."

Chen Pingan began to meditate inwardly.

With some seniors, there was no need to think too much.

Focus unwavering, Chen Pingan instinctively settled into a cross-legged position, his fists gently resting on his knees.

Sitting felt like his mind was drifting through countless ages, emerging from the endless cycle of the sun and moon.

Chen Chunan sat upright in the void, and upon hearing the scholar's insights, he smiled faintly.

Not only could Chen Chunan hear Chen Pingan's inner thoughts, but he could also easily draw out any ideas or notions Chen Pingan had, should he wish to.

Afterward, Xie Songhua and Shao Yunyan, having received word through their flying swords, arrived swiftly on their swords, breaking through countless waves and clouds, and found the "Wapan" ferry boat in the Mountain Water Cave, one after another welcomed by Chen Chunan into this realm of sun and moon.

The three jade purity sword immortals who arrived sequentially were all alike, showing no intention to draw their swords; they merely stood at their respective places, supporting Lu Zhi.

Mi Yu was more restrained, keeping a close watch on the battlefield. His refusal to intervene was to avoid complicating matters; as long as Lu Zhi maintained the upper hand, he would not strike.

The second to arrive, Shao Yunyan, true to his role as the owner of the Spring Fan Studio, directly began forging his sword using the abundant solar essence and lunar spirit present in the air.

Lastly, Xie Songhua, who entered this realm later, appeared far more relaxed compared to Mi Yu and Shao Yunyan. Upon entering, she glanced at the battlefield, deemed her assistance unnecessary, and began leisurely flying around on her sword.

This was a subtle indication of the different personalities among the sword immortals: Mi Yu seemed carefree, yet was actually the most restrained; Shao Yunyan was the most pragmatic and adept at calculations, while Xie Songhua's character was the most pure and free-spirited.

Chen Chunan said, "The situation is clear now. That ascendant demon has lost its true form, and the person from the border has been used as an external body for the Yang God to reside. The demon's hidden methods are a unique divine art, which is why it dared to approach the Sword Qi Great Wall. As long as this person does not stand on the city wall, even Chen Qingdu would not detect it. How did you discover it?"

Chen Pingan replied softly, "I placed three bets successively. First, I bet whether to leave the Summer Palace and follow a certain ferry boat away from the Inverted Mountain. Then I bet which ferry boat among those was more likely to be significant, and finally, I wagered whether you, old sir, would think I was playing games and be willing to come all the way from the Southern Posa continent. If you hadn’t come, even if I had guessed right on the first two, it would have been a wasted trip."

Chen Chunan laughed, "Then please elaborate. Don’t feel ashamed just because it has to do with 'gambling.' The hardest part of worldly knowledge is to articulate it well; making it accessible to others and relatable is even more difficult."

Just as Chen Pingan was about to speak, the ascendant demon crashed through Lu Zhi's sword strike, charging towards Chen Chunan and Chen Pingan.

The size of its dharma form loomed like a mountain overhead.

Yet, Chen Chunan did not even glance at it. He simply extended a hand and sent the half-formed ascendant demon, whose true form was hidden, crashing back into the battlefield. Not only did he strike it down, but its colossal body was also pressed into the golden sun, immersed in a sea of molten gold. Even when the demon roared in anger and soared thousands of feet into the air, it was still ensnared by those golden threads and harshly pulled back to the "earth."

Lu Zhi did not take the opportunity to strike either; she merely observed coldly, allowing the demon to escape and continue its confrontation.

Chen Chunan paid little mind to this.

The old scholar simply smiled, listening intently as the young man meticulously recounted the nuances of his three bets.

Back at the Summer Palace of the Sword Qi Great Wall, he tossed a small summer coin to decide whether to follow the "Wapan" ferry boat away from the Inverted Mountain. If it landed heads, he would do it; if tails, he would remain at the Summer Palace, waiting for the other party to take the initiative.

Previously, Chen Pingan had used a method of stopping and observing, albeit quite rudimentary, but it allowed him to discard a certain thought. As a result, the summer coin landed heads.

According to Chen Pingan's original plan, he should have stayed at the Summer Palace.

After some hesitation, he pressed down on the coin, prompting Guo Zhujiu to guess its outcome. Ultimately, Chen Pingan decided to leave the Sword Qi Great Wall.

Upon hearing this, Chen Chunan smiled and said, "So you initially wanted to determine your luck this way? If your luck was good, then you’d have to be cautious, and if it was poor, and you guessed incorrectly, there would be a chance for the opposite to occur?"

Chen Pingan nodded, "That’s right. I prefer not to engage in losing trades. I can forgo profit, but I absolutely cannot incur losses."

Chen Chunan laughed, "Continue."

Chen Pingan sought out the current figure of authority at the Inverted Mountain, a Daoist master he had encountered once before. Before the eldest disciple left, he had mentioned that after he drew his sword in the Jiao Long Gorge, this person had collected a significant number of dragon whiskers, benefiting greatly. "Junior brother, if you go find him about something, it shouldn't be difficult. If he refuses, just let him wait for my return to the Inverted Mountain and reason with him."

Additionally, with the spies placed by both the Sword Qi Great Wall and Cui Dongshan at the Inverted Mountain, when the last cross-continental ferry boat from the Spring Fan Studio departed, Chen Pingan obtained detailed records of all passengers boarding.

Before quietly returning to the Spring Fan Studio at the Inverted Mountain, Chen Pingan first gathered Lin Junbi, Xuan Can, and several other experts skilled in strategy and breaking the game from the Hidden Official lineage to help him sift through the most likely ten ferry boats that could cause unexpected incidents, including Wu Qiao, Tang Feiqian, and the "South Horn" ferry from Aiai continent, the "Wapan" from Fuyun continent, "Tai Gong" from Aiai continent, "Nishang" from the Immortal Islands, "Fuzhong" from Liuxia continent, one from both Southern and Northern Posa continents, and even the ferry from the Ding family of Old Dragon City.

Ironically, the greatest suspect could also be the one with the least suspicion.

At the outset, neither Chen Pingan nor Lin Junbi had thought that the Wapan ferry from the Mountain Water Cave was necessarily an insider hidden in the majestic realm.

Aside from selecting these ten ferry boats, there were also thirty-two suspicious ferry passengers.

Chen Chunan inquired, "That person from the border should be cautious and should not be among them."

Chen Pingan smiled, "Indeed, this person wasn’t listed initially. According to the original records, after leaving the Sword Qi Great Wall, the sword cultivator from the Shao Yuan dynasty of the Central Land, who is from the border, stayed in the Meihua Garden for a while before leaving the Inverted Mountain. However, it wasn’t with Yan Lu and Jiang Guancheng; instead, he chose to travel alone to Fuyun continent. The ferry boat that the sword immortal Lu Zhi and I initially boarded was Mi Yu’s 'Nishang.' After some investigation, we found no results, which was why we followed the Wapan ferry. After boarding mid-journey, I employed the simplest method, moving around to count the number of people, and discovered one extra person. Even so, I still dared not assert that a great demon was hidden on the ferry, nor could I claim the Mountain Water Cave had early ties with the wild realm."

Chen Chunan nodded, then humorously asked, "You didn’t choose to board the ferry following Xie Jianxian’s direction. Are you quite at ease with the Posa continent and Northern Julu continent?"

Chen Pingan shook his head, replying, "It’s more about trusting that a great demon’s mind is smart enough not to stir up trouble, not wanting to risk the advantageous situation of Tongye continent that was bought at the cost of two great demon lives."

Chen Chunan continued, "It seems you’re not worried that I might be angry about running around for nothing, just to speak of Tongye continent? Truly, you’re good at business."

Chen Pingan responded, "I sincerely request that you trust the Posa continent's insight just this once. The real gamble is that our Posa continent is the first and the greatest!"

Chen Chunan fell silent for a moment, then smiled with satisfaction, "Very well."

Meanwhile, Mi Yu continued to feign concern for Lu Zhi, with the great sun hanging in the sky, feeling as if it were within reach, the sheer heat making Mi Yu feel restless.

Shao Yunyan, seizing the opportunity, scooped up a handful of the golden lava that splattered outward, not daring to touch it directly, but carefully pouring it over his personal flying sword.

The osmanthus-carrying Xie Songhua asked loudly, "Old Scholar Chen, could you spare me some solar essence and lunar spirit? The kind I don’t have to return!"

Chen Chunan looked up and smiled, "Sword Immortal Xie, take as much as you like."

He glanced at the idle Mi Yu and said with a grin, "Sword Immortal Mi, could I borrow your sword for a moment?"

Mi Yu immediately removed his sword.

Chen Chunan reached out, grasped the sword, drew it from its sheath, and waved his sleeve, releasing a thick essence of moonlight. "This lunar spirit originally comes from the wild realm."

With his two fingers together, he gently stroked the sword’s blade, revealing an imperceptible groove. The rich moonlight flowed along his fingers, pouring into it.

Mi Yu's spirit swayed, nearly moving him to tears, and it was utterly sincere.

His personal sword's quality would undoubtedly be elevated, but more importantly, the cultured Chen Chunan personally helped him forge the sword! How could the sneaky Shao Yunyan, who forged his sword in a haphazard manner, compare? How could the forthright Xie Songhua, who asked for solar essence and lunar spirit, compare?

Chen Pingan shot a glance at Mi Yu.

The latter immediately understood, nodding in agreement. This was all thanks to the Hidden Official; he, Mi Yu, was most grateful for the kindness shown!

After helping Mi Yu complete the sword forging with the moonlight, Chen Chunan sheathed the sword.

The sword returned to Mi Yu in an instant.

Mi Yu cupped his fists and bowed, "Mi Yu thanks the cultured old sage."

Chen Chunan nodded and smiled, then turned to Chen Pingan, saying, "This matter was executed extremely well; ultimately, it was not the conduct of a gentleman."

Chen Pingan replied, "As of now, I’m not even a sage, so I’m certainly not a gentleman."

Chen Chunan chuckled, "You’re not unlike your teacher, who loves to cite titles. 'I’ve never been a sage or a gentleman.' 'You all forced this sage title upon me; did anyone ask if I was willing? Now that I am a sage, I’m terrified—what more do you want?'"

Chen Pingan remained silent.

Having acknowledged his teacher, he felt he should refrain from discussing the revered.

Chen Chunan sighed, "In Confucianism, one must study with rectitude and tranquility to illuminate virtue."

The old man gazed into the distance and fell into deep thought for a long while before saying slowly, "A sage’s thoughts should be thorough and meticulous. A gentleman’s words must be especially precise and detailed."

Chen Pingan was inspired and spoke out, "Cultivating strength, each punch and sword stroke should not miss the target, securing a foothold in reason. Cultivating the heart, only seeking the lofty, yet in the subtlety, one should inquire of their true self."

The old man did not comment on this.

The next moment, Chen Pingan found himself back in the cabin of the ferry.

He had been cast out into the void by Chen Chunan.

Bai Xi still stood in place.

In such a vast world, what could a mere Nascent Soul cultivator like him do? Even without obstruction, could he abandon the ferry to hide in the vast ocean? Or would he desperately rush to the Mountain Water Cave in Fuyun continent?

A Hidden Official, four sword immortals, and on top of that, the top figure of Southern Posa, Chen Chunan.

Bai Xi felt that even if he were in the Sword Qi Great Wall, he wouldn't necessarily survive among the wild realm's forces.

Chen Pingan smiled and asked, "Master Bai, how much time has passed?"

Bai Xi, seemingly ignoring the question, immediately said, "Lord Hidden Official, I am willing to atone for my mistakes! As long as I can live, I’ll do anything! I can testify against my ancestor’s collusion with the demon clans! I know all the resources of the Mountain Water Cave; I can offer them all to support the Sword Qi Great Wall…"

Chen Pingan lightly took a seat and interrupted him with a smile, "No need to rush. Everything can be set aside for the sake of the Hidden Official’s coin; let’s sit down and chat. There’s no hurry on how to make amends. Are you considering taking risks to capture me as a hostage, betting on the slim chance that the Hidden Official's realm is not high enough, so you can avoid the urgency?"

Bai Xi was drenched in sweat, his movements stiff, his expression dazed as he collapsed into a chair.

"Master Bai, that’s truly going too far."

Chen Pingan smiled, "If we’re talking about acting, you and I are kindred spirits. It’s a pity that you’re older but lack cultivation. You can compare your heart’s darkness, your realm, your resources, and everything else, but don’t ever compare this with me."

Suddenly, Bai Xi stood, his chair flying backward. As a Nascent Soul, he retreated a few steps and knelt, beginning to bow his head. "Lord Hidden Official, please save me!"

This was because the young Hidden Official was no longer alone; behind him stood the suddenly manifesting jade purity sword immortal, Mi Yu.

Chen Pingan poured himself a cup of tea, smiling as he asked, "Bring out your personal items, both private and from the sect, and remember to help me open them. If your sincerity is sufficient, I wouldn’t mind letting you gain something in this disaster, sitting in the first chair of the Mountain Water Cave. No matter my realm or background, you might still be confused, but you should be very clear about the kind of person I am; I always seek to maximize profit. This is your last chance, so cherish it."

After half a cup of tea, on the table before the young Hidden Official lay an ancient inkstone resembling a treasure chest from the Mountain Water Cave, and a fragrant fan, which was a personal item of the ferry's steward, along with many valuable items and celestial coins.

Some secrets of the Mountain Water Cave were also partially revealed by Bai Xi, but of course, he wouldn’t spill everything.

Bai Xi was not foolish.

Chen Pingan was even less so.

He took out a jade bamboo fan, lightly fanning himself while signaling Mi Yu to collect the personal and private items. If there was a hidden danger, Mi Yu could handle it. Even if he couldn’t entirely manage it, a Hidden Official at the lower realms shouldn’t have to bear the brunt of it.

Then, leaning back, Chen Pingan asked, "What are you waiting for? Get rid of him. Is he meant to be kept around for drinks or meals?"

Both Bai Xi and Mi Yu were startled.

Then, the world shifted again quietly.

Mi Yu slashed down with his sword, and it was remarkably smooth, comparable to being in the Sword Qi Great Wall, showing no trace of the pressure from the small realm, while the old Nascent Soul cultivator became somewhat sluggish.

This contrast, combined with the vast disparity between a jade purity sword immortal and a Nascent Soul cultivator, left no room for doubt.

Mi Yu's sword cleaved Bai Xi’s body in two, and not only that, but also split his golden core and the Nascent Soul in half.

However, just as Mi Yu was about to strike again, the young Hidden Official intervened, using a secret technique he had obtained from a business deal with Liu Zhimo at the Shujian Lake to bind the remnants of Bai Xi’s soul, gathering it in his palm while smiling, "If you ask me to save you, I will, so are you happy? What will your gratitude be?"

The suffering soul, barely able to hold back its cries, trembled and said, "Lord Hidden Official, you just need to speak; just make your request…"

Chen Pingan smiled and said, "I told you to be sincere, but you didn’t listen? What’s the outcome? Not very good, right? I’ll give you another chance; tell me the true secrets of the Mountain Water Cave, and you can live. You’re too high in realm for me to trust you as the next leader of the Mountain Water Cave. Right now, it’s perfect; your cultivation is so low that when you see me in the future, you’ll have to rely on celestial coins to get by."

The soul no longer dared to hide anything and revealed all the secret dealings of the Mountain Water Cave’s ancestor, as well as the infamous saying of "a cunning rabbit has three burrows, and treasures are scattered."

"Thank me with your death."

Chen Pingan nodded, clenched his fist, and crushed the frail soul with his strength. He then closed his folding fan and gently waved it to disperse the ethereal ashes of the soul, holding it to his chest, smiling, "Unexpected, isn’t it?"

Mi Yu was no longer surprised.

Chen Pingan stood, sheathing his folding fan, asking, "How much longer do you think Lu Zhi will take to slay that falsely titled ascendant demon? And is there any possibility of asking about the demon’s true form?"

Mi Yu looked troubled.

Who should he ask? Lu Zhi? She would hardly care to listen to him. Chen Chunan? Mi Yu didn’t have the face to do so.

Chen Pingan sighed, "Mi Yu, you really need to be more observant."

Mi Yu felt wronged.

Then Mi Yu’s curiosity piqued further; he surveyed his surroundings, noticing some signs. The sword cultivator at the upper fifth realm was indeed a sword immortal, and his insight was quite keen.

Was this the Hidden Official's personal flying sword?!

Chen Pingan retracted his personal flying sword, walking to the window.

Mi Yu sheathed his sword, standing guard nearby.

In the realm of sun and moon, the female sword immortal Lu Zhi battled fiercely with the ascendant demon.

In the cage-like small realm, Mi Yu had slain the Nascent Soul Bai Xi, and his soul was once again captured by Chen Pingan using a secret technique, then crushed with his fist.

The other qi cultivators aboard the Wapan ferry remained blissfully unaware of the unusual events happening around them.

Afterward.

The Wapan ferry continued its journey to Fuyun continent’s Mountain Water Cave, but it was now without a sneaky ascendant demon and with the boatmaster Bai Xi dead.

Lu Zhi joined them, while Chen Chunan did not accompany them but handed Lu Zhi a Confucian jade pendant.

Shao Yunyan was responsible for helping Lu Zhi deal with the aftermath of the Mountain Water Cave's chaos.

Though the chaos was indeed chaotic, the celestial coins were plentiful.

Shao Jianxian’s Spring Fan Studio could nominally receive a ten percent share.

However, the entire Spring Fan Studio had become the "private property" of the Hidden Official lineage, and even Shao Yunyan could not understand what that ten percent share really meant.

As for how to deal with the Mountain Water Cave, Chen Pingan had already clarified all the steps to Lu Zhi and Shao Yunyan.

Lu Zhi listened absentmindedly; anyway, with Shao Yunyan around, she planned to go into closed-door cultivation for a short while once she arrived at Fuyun continent.

She disliked these calculations of human hearts and was not skilled in them.

As for Xie Songhua, she would return to the Jiang Gaotai ferry to head to Aiai continent.

Before they parted ways, the young Hidden Official couldn’t help but chatter about the two children, prompting Xie Songhua to angrily ask if those two kids were their daughters.

Only then did the young Hidden Official fall silent.

Mi Yu found it amusing but dared not show it.

After all, people who could make the Hidden Official suffer were few and far between.

Chen Pingan and Mi Yu then boarded a talisman boat to return to the Inverted Mountain.

Chen Pingan stood at the bow of the ferry, glancing back at Mi Yu.

Sitting lazily at the stern, Mi Yu suddenly felt uneasy, wondering if another burden was about to fall on his shoulders.

Come, come, as long as Mi Da Jianxian furrows a brow, he won’t be the leader of the Hidden Official lineage!

Chen Pingan laughed, "After all the hustle and bustle, Shao Jianxian reaped a ten percent share of the Mountain Water Cave, Xie Jianxian repaid her favor, Lu Da Jianxian gained benefits in swordsmanship, along with that ascendant demon’s essence, and our Mi Jianxian’s sword quality has also improved. The personal and private items are also the collective gain of our Hidden Official lineage. It seems I’m the only one who has been running around for nothing?"

Mi Yu replied seriously, "Lord Hidden Official’s strategic planning and slaying of the ascendant demon is the foremost achievement, utterly deserved…"

Chen Pingan interrupted Mi Yu, clicking his tongue, "With your meager skills in flattery, if you were to go to my hometown, you wouldn’t even qualify as a named disciple, let alone a disciple."

Mi Yu felt heartbroken.

He had never been good at this; his path always relied on genuine feelings exchanged with beautiful women.

However, Mi Yu quickly made a feeble attempt to salvage, saying, "When I get there, you can just let me host the various fairies visiting the mountain. If there’s any slip-up, feel free to hold me accountable, Lord Hidden Official."

Chen Pingan smiled thinly, "Stay far away. The atmosphere in my mountain is already quite bizarre; even I, the mountain lord, can’t seem to reel it back in. With you around, wouldn’t your reputation go through the roof?"

Mi Yu felt utterly wronged.

After a moment of hesitation, he asked curiously, "Lord Hidden Official, why did you not accept the demon core that Lu Zhi offered? She truly didn’t want to keep it. According to the merit calculations of the Hidden Official lineage, this item should rightfully belong to you."

Chen Pingan sat down, gazing at the vast and boundless scenery of the rippling waters. "It’s not that I didn’t accept it; I did, but I asked Lu Zhi to pass it on to a friend in Southern Posa."

Mi Yu exclaimed, "Oh," suddenly realizing that obtaining an ascendant demon's core in the majestic realm was equivalent to acquiring a jade purity cultivator's glazed golden body? 

And this was called "nothing to worry about"?

Chen Pingan lightly tapped his palm with the closed fan, turning his head with a smile, "Hmm?"

Mi Yu immediately exclaimed, "Lord Hidden Official, you’re so selfless! You truly are a celestial among mortals. In all the tales of talented scholars and beautiful women, all the stories of supernatural beings and strange occurrences should replace 'the exiled immortal' with 'Chen Pingan.'"

Mi Yu felt he was gradually coming into his own; although he still did not dare to battle with Guo Zhujiu, the Hidden Official’s direct disciple, he should now be able to compete with Gu Jianlong on this matter.

Chen Pingan turned back, continuing to gaze ahead, and after a long silence, he suddenly said, "Mi Yu, I’m happy that we’ve turned from strangers into friends."

Mi Yu was taken aback for a moment, then finally nodded, "It’s an honor to meet Chen Pingan."

After a moment, Chen Pingan asked, "As a parting gift, what did you write on the folding fan you gave to that female Nascent Soul cultivator from the Central Land?"

Mi Yu’s smile became awkward. "Such trivial romantic sentiments would only make the Hidden Official laugh at me; it’s better not to mention it."

Chen Pingan insisted, "Tell me."

When it came to dealing with women, Mi Yu’s cultivation level was quite impressive.

Mi Yu hesitated, "Then I’ll truly be embarrassing myself?"

After all, this young Hidden Official had once been the shopkeeper, overseeing the records of the Hundred Sword Immortal and the Bi Sword Immortal, along with a plethora of fan inscriptions. Mi Yu was likely the most dedicated sword immortal in the Sword Qi Great Wall, diligently researching numerous ways, especially the fan inscriptions that delighted women. He had inquired about them and copied them down, studying them thoroughly, and felt he had gained immensely.

Deep down, Mi Yu also believed that his fan inscriptions should at least have the skill level of a shopkeeper.

Since they were on the ferry with no outsiders around, he figured it was a good opportunity to share without losing face.

On one side of the fan, he had written, "Pity the one before my eyes, yet I smell the osmanthus. I surely grow thin from this, as the shame belongs to my lord."

On the other side, he inscribed, "Walking, I think of you; sitting, I think of you; not being able to walk, sitting is difficult. Missing you, not seeing you, I drink and laugh; how few are the days of life."

Chen Pingan remained silent for a long time after hearing this.

Finally, he couldn’t help but shout, "Get out and fly your sword!"

He genuinely felt that in the realm of love and romance, where talent was more important than cultivation, he would never catch up to Mi Yu’s shadow.

The wronged Mi Yu had no choice but to get up, disgruntled, as he obediently left the talisman boat and began to fly away in the distance.

Upon reaching the Inverted Mountain, he first visited the Spring Fan Studio. This residence was unique among the four private residences because it was entirely a refined item. From its construction, Shao Yunyan had set up numerous formations and talismans, which meant that from the very beginning, the Spring Fan Studio had not truly settled within the largest mountain seal of this realm. In contrast, the more resource-consuming Yuan Rou Mansion had not considered this, while the Meihua Garden had no chance of being refined.

Shao Yunyan handed over a crucial treasure that served as the core of the great formation to Chen Pingan.

After confirming the details, Chen Pingan departed with Mi Yu from the Spring Fan Studio.

Yan Ming and Nalan Caihuan stayed behind in the residence, responsible for receiving other ferry managers arriving from the eight continents.

Mi Yu would also remain, but he still needed to escort Chen Pingan to the connecting gates between the two great realms, curiously asking, "Why don’t we use the old gate closer to the Spring Fan Studio? The elder Zhang Lu stationed there and that book-loving little Taoist boy seem quite interesting."

Chen Pingan merely replied with a noncommittal "Mm," without further explanation.

Mi Yu had only asked casually, and he didn’t think much of it.

After sending the Hidden Official to the gate, Mi Yu needed to return to the Spring Fan Studio. He was familiar with many of the female boatmasters and ferry cultivators; unfortunately, they were all acquaintances without fate.

Upon entering the hall of the Summer Palace, everyone looked up.

Guo Zhujiu was the first to speak, "Master, how many ascendant demons did you slay this time?"

Chen Pingan, feeling somewhat fatigued, sat on the threshold, "Just one."

Guo Zhujiu blinked, "There really was one? Master, I don’t know how to explain the next part!"

The sword immortal Chou Miao looked toward Chen Pingan.

Chen Pingan nodded and smiled, "There really was."

Chou Miao clasped his fists but didn’t say anything.

The first group of three sword cultivators who had gone out to slay from the city wall—Chou Miao, Dong Budie, and Deng Liang—had already returned.

Since Mi Yu had gone with Chen Pingan to the Spring Fan Studio, only Pang Yuanji and Lin Junbi had gone out to fight.

Chen Pingan said, "It’s not as comfortable here; I’ll take a little break, so you all carry on."

The people in the room busied themselves once more.

Even Guo Zhujiu, who was usually persistent, refrained from seeking out her master for a chat.

Now, the Hidden Official lineage was gradually forming several small factions.

Lin Junbi and Pang Yuanji got along well. Pang Yuanji was less spirited lately, doing tasks or occasionally playing chess with Lin Junbi, seeking guidance.

Pang Yuanji learned chess quickly. Outside the chessboard, Lin Junbi was growing rapidly, and all the other members of the Hidden Official lineage noticed and paid attention.

The foreign sword cultivator Song Gaoyuan got along well with Luo Zhenyi, Xu Ning, and Chang Taiqing.

Deng Liang enjoyed chatting with Dong Budie every few days; even the blind could tell that this former wild cultivator, who had eventually ascended to the sect's roster as a Nascent Soul sword cultivator, had his aspirations.

However, it was evident that Dong Budie had no interest in Deng Liang, and anyone could see it.

Privately, Chen Pingan had once joked with Deng Liang, saying, "I’m a good brother of Chen Sanqiu; if you keep this up, I’ll pull Chen Sanqiu into the Hidden Official lineage."

Deng Liang laughed, saying it was fine, "I’m a Nascent Soul sword cultivator; that young master Chen is still at the Golden Core bottleneck. As long as the Hidden Official doesn’t show favoritism, I guarantee he’ll come in standing tall and leave horizontally."

Then Deng Liang added, "Even without discussing realms, just in terms of drinking, young master Chen is no match for me."

Gu Jianlong, Wang Xinshui, along with Cao Gun and Xuan Can, formed a cohesive group of four guardians, progressing and retreating together, and they particularly liked to follow Guo Zhujiu’s lead. Whenever Guo Zhujiu employed the sect's absolute skill, the remaining four would follow suit.

Ultimately, these four young individuals were those closest to the Hidden Official and could be shameless.

Today was an exception; in truth, the achievement of slaying a hidden ascendant demon was so shocking that Gu Jianlong and the others dared not speak.

Lin Junbi and Xuan Can were both masters of chess, often playing together.

Chen Pingan would also assist Xuan Can in strategizing. Xuan Can, being somewhat forgetful, often suffered defeat despite having received the Hidden Official’s guidance repeatedly.

Guo Zhujiu would complain about why Xuan Can couldn’t keep up with her master’s thoughts, wasting the Hidden Official’s golden advice that could secure victory.

Gu Jianlong and Wang Xinshui, not understanding chess, preferred to make a ruckus. One would cheer for Xuan Can, while the other would chatter about Lin Junbi, calling it a strategy of psychological warfare.

Pang Yuanji often sought a quiet spot in the Summer Palace to daydream alone.

Chou Miao would offer sword technique guidance to all the younger cultivators, including Deng Liang and Song Gaoyuan, as long as they were willing to ask. As a sword immortal, Chou Miao was always willing to teach patiently.

Dong Budie would occasionally drag Luo Zhenyi along to discuss female matters; originally, Luo Zhenyi, who often maintained a serious demeanor, now displayed a hint of gentleness in her brows and eyes.

Guo Zhujiu was the least factional among them; she could ask Chou Miao for sword skills, chat with Pang Yuanji, and preferred to join Dong Budie and Luo Zhenyi, engaging in lively discussions, leading to countless amusing incidents, from bumping heads on tables to hitting walls, ending with no exception.

Chen Pingan viewed all this as a good thing.

A person’s state of mind cannot always be tense; it requires a balance of relaxation to endure.

Within the Hidden Official lineage, while everyone performed their roles, they complemented one another, without missing gaps, pooling strengths to make up for shortcomings. They had already established a structured approach, making headway.

Chen Pingan no longer expected these sword cultivators to do better, but he thought, as the Hidden Official, sometimes, one still had to act like a villain.

If it came to the craft of speaking in veiled tones, using pretty words to convey sharp-edged content, Chen Pingan was truly the master, far surpassing the skilled Gu Jianlong.

Of course, this was predicated on hitting the mark; otherwise, if one only ridiculed, it would backfire.

Chen Pingan recalled something and tossed the personal and private items obtained from the Mountain Water Cave's Wapan ferry to Guo Zhujiu, smiling, "This is extra profit."

Then Chen Pingan detailed the entire process of this journey, glossing over what couldn’t be disclosed. For instance, how he had drawn out many of the Mountain Water Cave’s secrets from a Nascent Soul boatmaster, and how he had ensured the killing while preserving the inkstone and fan, specifically knowing how to open the doors.

Guo Zhujiu cleared her table, her eyes shining as she spat into her palm and rubbed her hands together, then began to count the celestial treasures and the pile of celestial coins within the personal and private items.

Dong Budie laughed, "Lord Hidden Official, are you telling us that you have a personal item called the treasure pot?"

Earlier, during their return to the Summer Palace, they had brought back over one hundred celestial treasures from the Spring Fan Studio.

This time, leaving the Inverted Mountain, they brought back two treasures from the mountain, along with a hefty amount of wealth hidden within.

Guo Zhujiu, without looking up, huffed, "It’s only because my master is righteous and deliberately refrained from using his powers; otherwise, if he were to travel to Southern Posa today and then to Central Land tomorrow, he could have dragged back mountains of gold and silver."

Chen Pingan laughed, "Gold and silver can’t be moved, but I did bring you a worthless snowball. You can handle your tasks first; later, we can make a few smaller snowmen."

From his personal items, Chen Pingan took out the large snowball.

In other places of the Sword Qi Great Wall, snowballs were hard to keep, but in the Summer Palace, if placed under the big tree, it would likely last for several days without concern.

Guo Zhujiu was overjoyed, "Master, you’re giving me a gift?! Luckily, the senior sister can’t see this; otherwise, she might want to swap with me for senior sister and junior sister!"

Chen Pingan’s expression softened with a smile, "Take care; your senior sister holds grudges. Her little ledger is something I don’t even get to see."

Guo Zhujiu sat down, swaying her shoulders left and right, mimicking her senior sister, feeling incredibly joyful, at a loss for words.

Without a small gong or drum nearby, she felt a twinge of regret.

Then everyone in the room saw the young Hidden Official, bending over with his back to them, starting to build a small snowman in the sweltering summer heat of the Summer Palace.

Chen Pingan suddenly said, "Regarding the ascendant demon 'Border,' do not hold any grievances against Lin Junbi; he has nothing to do with this. The other party is scheming to become Lin Junbi’s senior brother, which has great implications."

Chou Miao laughed, "We were all waiting for Lord Hidden Official to say this."

Indeed, many people breathed a sigh of relief.

Chen Pingan continued, "By the way, the treasures from the Mountain Water Cave, we Hidden Official lineage will not be splitting the spoils."

A hush fell over the room.

Guo Zhujiu clapped her hands on the table, shouting that it was outrageous, effectively being the only one to defend the Hidden Official.

Gu Jianlong and Wang Xinshui were the loudest, whistling vigorously.

Even Luo Zhenyi began to complain alongside Dong Budie.

Xuan Can and Cao Gun sighed deeply, lamenting that their meager and stingy lives were unbearable.

Chen Pingan laughed heartily, "It seems this truly has been lost."

Guo Zhujiu gleefully said, "You lot are all a bit dim-witted."

Chen Pingan waved his hand, "Come and take a look at the snowman I built."

Guo Zhujiu jumped up, quickly grabbed her small bamboo box, swaggering over the threshold, and plopped down. After a moment of astonished silence, she timidly asked, "Master, who is this? It’s my senior sister, right?"

The snowman had two slanted bamboo leaves stuck on its large head, striking a pose, holding a bamboo branch, appearing foolish and unrefined.

Chen Pingan smiled, "It's a gift for you; place it on the table."

Guo Zhujiu frowned thoughtfully.

She glanced at Dong Budie, who lifted a hand to gently press down on the table.

Guo Zhujiu had no choice but to hold the small snowman, obediently returning to her seat, following her master’s orders, placing the snowman on the table while turning it around, facing Dong Budie.

Chen Pingan clapped his hands and stood up.

He thought of the two children who had already been taken to Aiai continent by Xie Songhua; in the future, Wei Jin, Shao Yunyan, and all the sword immortals returning home from the Sword Qi Great Wall would bring along one or two young sword cultivators who were not yet high in realm.

Dandelions, drifting away with the wind to distant lands.

He hoped that these children from the Sword Qi Great Wall would one day become individuals like Liu Xianyang and Chen Pingan, journeying far from the Li Pearl Cave, and perhaps even live better and more prosperous lives.

*(End of Chapter)*
